Reichstag Fire Case 54

French Newspapers Publish a Shocking Document

Proving Goebbels and Göring Conspired

(Paris) Today's Paris Daily publishes a shocking document with the handwritten signature of the late Berlin Stormtroopers Commander Ernst and countersigned by two people. It was addressed to Dr. Brandigt of Sweden. Ernst stated that it should not be published unless he died violently. The document proves that Propaganda Minister Goebbels and Prussian Prime Minister Göring were both accomplices in the burning of the Reichstag on February 27 of this year. The document cleared Hitler of everything, saying that he was completely unaware. The gist of the document is that the Stormtroopers initially discussed with Generals Goebbels and Göring to pretend that the Communists were plotting to assassinate the Prime Minister in order to damage the reputation of the Communist Party and consolidate the power of the National Defense Party. This plan was not implemented because everyone advocated setting fire to the Reichstag. Göring supplied flammable materials such as nitrate and sulfur. He (Ernst) carried them through the tunnel of the Prussian Prime Minister's Office to the Great Hall of the Reichstag and placed them in the hall, which spontaneously burned half an hour later. As for the Dutchman Lubbe, who was later sentenced to death in this case, he was weak-willed. Although he believed he was acting alone, he was actually used to cover up other people's ears and eyes. It was agreed at the time that half an hour after the Stormtroopers serving in the Reichstag withdrew, Lubbe would set fire in the Reichstag's auditorium. After the Reichstag fire, Lubbe and five others were arrested and charged with arson. This case caused worldwide shock. The Leipzig Higher Court interrogated the case for a long time and sentenced Lubbe to death on December 3, 1933, and acquitted the other four. Lubbe was executed on January 10 of this year. During the purge movement in June of this year, Hitler accused Ernst of disloyalty to the party, and he and many other Stormtroopers leaders were shot. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

German Government Controls National Banking Industry 58

Authorizing the Minister of Economic Affairs with Dictatorial Power Over Capital

(Berlin) The German Cabinet today passed several economic laws to tighten the control of Minister of Economic Affairs Hjalmar Schacht over Germany's capital resources. Schacht has now become Germany's capital dictator. One of the most important new laws limits all business dividends to no more than six percent. If there is a surplus, it must be deposited in cash in the discount bank as a loan. This reserve must be used for domestic relief and construction and cannot be withdrawn within four years. (National Telegram, 5th)

(Berlin) The Cabinet meeting recently passed several important financial and economic bills: ㈠ Revised the current regulations on the securities market and the financial market, stipulating the establishment of a control bureau to manage national banks and trust institutions. From now on, all securities interest may not exceed 6%. Any amount exceeding this number will be included in the government bond fund. In other words, although this fund should be returned to the original owner after four years in the regulations, in practice, the government will withdraw the net profit from industry and commerce within four years. ㈡ Stipulates that the copyright enjoyed by writers, musicians, and sculptors, originally set at 30 years, is extended to 50 years. ㈢ Stipulates the state's control over the prices of daily necessities, which also applies to the prices of industrial products. In addition, the government has decided to cut 12 securities exchanges, allowing only four to continue operating. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

However, railway stocks have been purchased recently, which can be regarded as a very constructive thing. Judging from the market situation, market prices will continue to rise. The rebound trend of yesterday seems to have slightly expanded today.

Hebei Provincial Government to Move Back to Baoding Within the Year 106

Government Headquarters Selected as the Cao Family Garden

Joint Office Work to Begin After the Move to Baoding

Beiping Communication: The issue of the Hebei Provincial Government moving to Baoding has been largely decided to be implemented on New Year's Day next year. Joint office work will also be implemented on the same day. The abolishment of bureaus and merger of sections in various counties under its jurisdiction was decided at the previous administrative conference convened by the Hebei Provincial Government to be implemented on New Year's Day next year. Except for the Public Security Bureau, whose name will remain unchanged to take special responsibility, the rest will be changed to sections. Regarding the Finance Bureau, it has been decided to be uniformly called the Second Section. The various details are recorded below:

Motivation for Moving to Baoding 107

The idea of the Hebei Provincial Government moving to Baoding has been brewing for a long time. Baoding was formerly the capital of Zhili Province and one of the important towns in North China. At that time, the prosperity of Baoding surpassed that of other provincial capitals. Later, due to changing times and circumstances, it was moved to Tianjin and then to Beiping, and then back to Tianjin. Recently, the authorities have considered that Hebei Province has become the forefront of national defense. For the sake of convenient control, it seems more appropriate to move back to Baoding. Moreover, Baoding is located in the center of Hebei Province, backed by heavy mountains in the west and converging rivers in the east, guarding the throat of Shanxi and controlling the key to Shandong and Henan. Its importance is evident. Huang Fu, the Chairman of the Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, after returning to office from the north a few days ago, in addition to summoning Chairman Yu Xuezhong of Hebei to discuss the matter, also telegraphed the central government to suggest it. The residents of Baoding were deeply supportive of this idea and encouraged and welcomed it. Since the province was moved, the market conditions in Baoding have been declining to the extreme. If the provincial government can move back, prosperity can be expected and the local economy can be revived. Therefore, the people of the area wish for the Hebei Provincial Government to move back to Baoding. Before the reorganization of the Hebei Provincial Government, the Cao Family Garden in Baoding had already started repairs in preparation for its application at that time, and it was decided to prepare for the move after the executive Yuan's regular meeting passed the proposal. According to reliable sources, the Hebei Provincial Government will work in Baoding from New Year's Day next year. In any case, the move will begin within the year, with the goal of completing the move before the New Year.

Joint Office Work 108

The Hebei Provincial Government has long been prepared for joint office work. In addition to sending personnel to various provinces that have already implemented joint office work for inspection and as a reference, Chairman Yu Xuezhong personally inspected the results of joint office work in the two provinces of Jiangxi and Hubei when he went to Ganzhou and Wuhan to visit Jiang and Zhang. After returning to Tianjin, he ordered the various departments to propose measures. Later, due to the small size of the government building in Tianjin, it could not be realized immediately, so it was temporarily shelved. Since the province had the brewing of moving to Baoding, Yu sent personnel to Baoding to survey and find a government building for use. The Cao Family Garden was selected, and workers were sent to repair it. The garden was built by Cao Kun when he was stationed in Baoding. The garden is vast and there are many houses, which is very suitable for the joint office work of various departments. The joint office work measures can also be submitted for discussion and voting at the provincial government's regular meeting in the short term. Its realization period is now set for New Year's Day next year, and it is unlikely to change.

Abolishment of Bureaus in Various Counties 109

The finances of Hebei Province have been stretched and extremely difficult for the past three years due to various losses from disaster relief. Since the central government decided to abolish miscellaneous taxes, it has felt increasingly unable to sustain itself. The compensation given by the central government is limited in number. If it is not remedied by further austerity measures, there is no complete solution. At the previous administrative conference, it was resolved that county governments should uniformly abolish bureaus and merge sections to save public funds. The Hebei Provincial Government and various departments were to issue orders to their subordinate county bureaus to prepare for completion within this year and implement them uniformly from New Year's Day next year. However, because the public security bureaus in various counties are responsible for maintaining public order, the public security bureaus will retain their names in order to facilitate administration. All other bureaus will be uniformly called sections. The Finance Bureau will be renamed the Second Section. The section chiefs will go to the county government to work on time every day. With this method, the county government's operating expenses can be saved by about one-third, and its administrative efficiency will be better than submitting documents back and forth. (4th)

British Minister Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen Arrives in Guangzhou 110

Provincial and Municipal Governments Host Welcome Banquet

British Envoy to Stay in Guangdong for Three Days Before Going to Hong Kong

Guangzhou Communication: British Minister to China, Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen, went south a few days ago to inspect British expatriates in various ports in South China. He arrived in Guangzhou on the afternoon of November 22 aboard the HMS "Mauritius".

The military and political authorities of Guangdong Province sent representatives to board the ship to welcome him. Because Knatchbull-Hugessen was tired from the voyage, he decided to go ashore the next day. Only the British Consul General in Guangdong, Mr. Philip, disembarked that day for a private meeting with Knatchbull-Hugessen. At 9:00 a.m. on the 23rd, Knatchbull-Hugessen, accompanied by Counselor Bielese and British Consul General Philip, took a car from Shamian to formally visit Governor Lin Yun'gai of Guangdong Province. In advance, in addition to sending personnel to Shamian to receive him, the Provincial Government also sent police detectives to protect him along the way. In front of the Provincial Government, guards of honor and a Western orchestra were arranged. Governor Lin Yun'gai was waiting at the second gate of the Provincial Government. When Knatchbull-Hugessen arrived, the ceremony was performed. The national anthems of China and Britain were played alternately. After the music stopped, Governor Lin accompanied Knatchbull-Hugessen to inspect the guards of honor for a week, and then held a meeting in the Western-style flower hall, where they talked to each other for about 20 minutes. Knatchbull-Hugessen then bid farewell and went to the Guangzhou Municipal Government to visit Mayor Liu Jiwen. He arrived at the Municipal Government at 10:30 a.m., met with Liu for a while, and then returned to the British Concession in Shamian for rest. At 3:00 p.m. that afternoon, Governor Lin Yun'gai of the Provincial Government went to the British Consulate in Shamian to return Knatchbull-Hugessen's visit. At 3:30 p.m., Mayor Liu Jiwen also arrived to return the visit. At 7:00 p.m., the Provincial Government hosted a banquet to entertain them, which was attended by Governor Lin Yun'gai, military and political figures such as Chen Jitang, and the heads of various departments of the Provincial Government. Foreign guests included Envoy Xu, Knatchbull-Hugessen, his wife Lady Knatchbull-Hugessen, British Counselor Bielese, British Consul General Philip, and Consul Huan Daer. During the banquet, Governor Lin delivered a speech, saying that his colleagues were honored by Knatchbull-Hugessen's visit to the province. The diplomatic relations between China and Britain have always been cordial, and Hong Kong and Guangzhou are particularly close in history and geography. Now that Your Excellency has come south, we have been able to receive valuable advice. We believe that the friendship between China and Britain will be further enhanced. After the speech, he raised his glass to Knatchbull-Hugessen and his wife, and wished the United Kingdom a prosperous future. Then Knatchbull-Hugessen stood up to respond and left happily at about 9:00 p.m. On the morning of the 24th, Knatchbull-Hugessen and the British Consul General and others visited famous scenic spots in Guangzhou and visited new construction projects. The provincial and municipal governments sent special commissioners to guide the tour, including the Haizhu Iron Bridge, the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall, the Tomb of the 72 Martyrs of Huanghuagang, the Henan Silk Weaving Factory, and the Xicun Cement Factory. They returned at about 12:00 p.m. At 8:00 p.m. that evening, the Municipal Government held a banquet to welcome Knatchbull-Hugessen, which was attended by the consuls of Germany, the United States, Norway, and Denmark stationed in Guangzhou, as well as the Postal Commissioner and the Tax Commissioner. During the banquet, Mayor Liu Jiwen delivered a welcome speech, saying that Guangzhou was the earliest port for trade. Among the cities in China, it has a close relationship with Britain's commerce in the Far East. For example, the distance between Guangdong and Hong Kong is only more than 300 li, and it takes only one day to travel from morning to evening. The distance from Singapore is only six or seven days by water. Business is closely related. Many British people operate or reside in Guangzhou. Chinese and British people have always had harmonious and cooperative feelings, so the diplomatic relations between China and Britain are becoming increasingly close. This is something we are pleased to see. We hope that this phenomenon will be maintained forever by the Chinese and British people. We are most honored to be able to gather together with Your Excellency this time, and we ask you to join us in raising a glass to the friendship between China and Britain. After the speech, Knatchbull-Hugessen returned the courtesy and then shook hands and bid farewell. At 10:00 a.m. on the 25th, the Municipal Government sent personnel to accompany Knatchbull-Hugessen and others to visit the Huangpodong scenic spot and the new campus of Sun Yat-sen University in Shipai. They returned to Shamian in the afternoon. Knatchbull-Hugessen dined at the British Consulate, and then left Guangzhou on the original ship at 6:00 p.m. that afternoon, heading to Hong Kong for a short stay before returning north. (Late November 25)

Ganzhou Province Celebrates剿匪 [Communist Suppression] Success 111

The Entire Province Displays Joyful Scenes

Nanchang Citizens Parade with Lanterns

Nanchang Communication: Jiangxi Province, from the 16th year of the Republic [1927] to the present, has groaned under the terror of the Reds for a total of eight years. During the era of rampant Communist bandits, among the eighty-one counties, the truly safe areas numbered no more than four or five. The various forces of Zhu [De], Mao [Zedong], Peng [Dehuai], Lin [Biao], and Luo [Ronghuan] had three times spied on Nanchang, twice reaching the West Mountains area near the city suburbs. The situation was precarious. Now, having stepped onto the broad road to recovery, the delight and jubilation are naturally a unanimous expression throughout the province, as Jiangxi, with the Central Government and Chairman Chiang [Kai-shek] devoting their full efforts to post-disaster recovery and reconstruction, will have all construction efforts centered on it, becoming a model. Misfortune may be a blessing in disguise; finding a cure through illness. This is what the people of Jiangxi privately rejoice in. Therefore, after Ruijin and Huichang were captured, and the provincial territory was restored to its complete and unbroken state, the Preparatory Office of Various Circles for Comforting Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Comforting the 剿匪 [Communist Suppression] Soldiers, Wounded and Sick Officers and Soldiers, and Compatriots in the Recovered Areas, initiated a large-scale celebration. Since the 30th of last month, Party and national flags have fluttered and danced throughout the city, and every household has been decorated with colorful red lanterns, creating a brilliant scene of peace and prosperity. On the 1st of this month, a celebration and comforting rally was held in Yuzhang Park, attended by over 1,800 representatives from various circles. It was also resolved to raise donations to establish a 剿匪 [Communist Suppression] Memorial Hall, and to petition the Central Government to allocate funds to establish a Disabled Soldiers' Factory, among five proposals. After the meeting, entertainment was held at the Changxin Grand Theater to share the joy. The 3rd was the last day of the celebration. Around 4 p.m. in the evening, a lantern parade was held at the public stadium. More than 10,000 people from various organs and groups participated in the parade in organized teams with lanterns. Starting at 5 p.m., all the lanterns, in order to comply with the principles of the New Life Movement, sought beauty in simplicity. The lanterns of the provincial government and departments were all oval-shaped and white, extremely clean and tidy. The lanterns of the provincial party headquarters were in the shape of a shield, containing a sense of self-defense. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau had lanterns depicting figures playing drums and blowing trumpets, showing the intention of joyful encouragement, preceded by lanterns with the heads of Zhu [De] and Mao [Zedong], as a sign of the capture and beheading of Zhu and Mao. Other examples included the "Capture of Red Bandits" lantern of the Municipal Martial Arts Hall, the automobile lanterns of the Transportation Corps, costumed propaganda, and the colorful displays of various industries, businesses, schools, and other sectors, all striving for novelty and beauty while still adhering to the principles of simplicity and plainness. The lantern procession passed through Huanhu Road North, through Zhangshuxia, past Yuzhang Park, into Desheng Road, turned onto Zhongshan Road, and circled back to Huanhu Road to return to the stadium. The procession was orderly, and the spectators along the way were like walls. It only dispersed at 8 p.m. In addition, the five proposals passed by the Celebration and Comforting Rally of Various Circles have been telegraphed: (1) Telegram to Nanjing to comfort Chairman Chiang Kai-shek; (2) Telegram to military hospitals throughout the country to comfort the wounded officers and soldiers who were suppressed by the Red Army; (3) Telegram to Ruijin, Huichang, Shicheng, Xingguo, Ningdu, and Guangchang to comfort the compatriots in the recovered areas; (4) Telegram to Beijing to support the Fifth Plenary Session; (5) Telegram to various places and circles to request donations to relieve refugees in bandit-stricken areas. (4th)

Anhui Rice Exports Suffer 112

|No Transactions in Guangzhou, Chaozhou, Yantai, or Ningbo|

Wuhu Communication: Wuhu is the area where rice and grain from southern Anhui converge. The annual exports are nearly ten million shi [a unit of dry measure]. There are more than 200 rice businesses in the whole port, roughly divided into three categories: rice firms, rice shops, and rice mills. Rice shops are those that buy and sell on behalf of customers, transfer and export, and collect commissions, as well as collect rice and grain on their own for transportation and sale to other places. Rice firms are divided into four gangs: Guangzhou, Chaozhou, Yantai, and Ningbo. They specialize in buying bulk quantities from rice mills and rice shops and transporting them to Guangzhou, Chaozhou, Yantai, Ningbo and other places. Rice mills sell rice that they hull themselves locally, or supply it to the people for food. According to statistics, the value of rice and grain exported from Wuhu each year reaches 10 million yuan. This year, since the provincial government promulgated the method of requisitioning grain for disaster relief, the rice market has been even more depressed. The Guangzhou, Chaozhou, Yantai, and Ningbo gangs have had hardly any transactions to speak of. As for rice mills and rice shops, they only have sporadic transactions. Recently, the market price for the best quality is nine yuan seven or eight jiao [monetary unit] per shi, and the secondary quality is eight yuan eight or nine jiao, which is more than three yuan per shi higher than two months ago. In addition, Wuhu produces the most glutinous rice, about 50,000 shi per year, followed by Nanling and Xuancheng, about 30,000 shi per year. Sales are also large in Yantai, Ningbo, Guangzhou, and Chaozhou. However, according to statistics from relevant authorities, this year's exports have been greatly reduced. Miscellaneous grains such as wheat and barley were originally mostly produced in northern Anhui, and Anqing also produced a lot. The annual production in counties near Wuhu is only about 160,000 to 170,000 shi. In addition to supplying the local Yixin Flour Mill, most of it is transported and sold to Tianjin, Shanghai, Jinan and other places. Rapeseed is also a major commodity among the miscellaneous grains produced in southern Anhui. Xuancheng, Wuhu, Wuwei, Hexian, Hanshan, Nanling, and Dangtu account for no less than one million shi. Hundreds of thousands of shi are transshipped from Wuhu to Shanghai every year, mostly bought by Japan. (4th)

Fire in the North Gate Intersection of Nanhui 113

Around midnight on the 4th, a fire suddenly broke out in the wood shed behind the Taihetang Pharmacy near the North Gate Intersection in the city. In an instant, it burst through the roof, and the firelight illuminated the sky. Drums were immediately sounded to call for help. Fire brigades rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm to pour water and extinguish the fire. Magistrate Yuan also led the security team and the entire Public Security Bureau to the scene to supervise the rescue and maintain order. However, since the location was in the city streets, it was difficult to fetch water for firefighting, and the shops and houses were closely connected, so there was a tendency for the fire to spread rapidly. Fortunately, the firefighters bravely dismantled the buildings of Guangfumao Grocery Store and Sanjin Socks Factory on both sides of the pharmacy, which allowed the fire to be extinguished. However, the pharmacy building was completely burned down, and the facade of Renji Sauce Garden on the opposite side was also scorched. Fortunately, it did not spread. The total loss of the stores is estimated to be about five to six thousand taels of silver.

Taicang Three-Life Case: Steaming Bones for Examination 114

The three-life case of intentional injury resulting in death of Chen Ajin of Shuangfeng, Lu Aquan of Zhitang, and Mo Alan of Shatou, which shook the whole county, should be opened for examination, bones being steamed, in order to clarify the facts, because of doubts about the injuries of the victims. The county government has specially submitted a request to the High Court to send an forensic examiner to Taicang for examination. Subsequently, the High Court issued an instruction to Xuan Fang, a forensic examiner of the Wuxian District Court, who is experienced in examining corpses, to consult with the county government. After receiving the order, the county government consulted with the Wuxian District Court. The president of the District Court promptly approved the letter. The forensic examiner Xuan arrived in Taicang on the first day and immediately began preparing the necessary instruments. On the third day, the county government sent police to Shuangfeng to transport Chen Ajin's coffin to Taicang. It was decided to start steaming the bones in the City God Temple in the city on the sixth day. After the examination of Chen's corpse is completed, the corpses of Lu and Mo will be examined.

New Director of Public Security Bureau of Suzhou Arrives in Suzhou 115

A series of robberies have occurred in Suzhou. Except for the capture of Qian Dehua and five others, the rest have not yet been solved. The provincial authorities are quite dissatisfied with this. Wang Bolin, the director of the special Public Security Bureau, was transferred to the province, and his vacant position was filled by Zhang Hanwei, a police inspector of the Civil Affairs Department. Zhang was inspecting police affairs in Shanghai when he received the appointment. After receiving the telegram, he returned to the province the day before yesterday to thank him for his appointment. He arrived in Suzhou at 5 p.m. yesterday and will take over his post at the bureau today or tomorrow.

Cigarette Boat Encountered Robbers in Dongshan 116

Shanghai Huapin Cigarette Company hired a boat the day before yesterday and sent Zhang Fukun and others to transport cigarettes to Dongshan and other villages to sell them. Unexpectedly, when the boat passed through the Daquegang area of Dong Houshan, it suddenly encountered a bandit boat that went to rob them. They were robbed of about five or six hundred yuan worth of silver dollars, cigarettes, clothes and other items. The bandits fled towards the East Tai Lake area.

Wuxi Drug Pellet Trafficker Sentenced 117

The Ninth Sub-Precinct of the Public Security Bureau directly under the jurisdiction of the Public Security Bureau arrested Hu Litang, a drug pellet trafficker, on the 17th of July this year in the middle of the road near Rongxiang. He was transferred to the General Bureau for interrogation. According to his confession, the drug pellets were bought from Dong Bifu at No. 22, Xishuiguan. Subsequently, Director Chen ordered the Inspection Department to arrest Dong and hand him over to the county government, which transferred him to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command for review. On the 20th of last month, Military Judge Zhou Shiqing sentenced the criminal in court in accordance with the Regulations on Strictly Prohibiting Highly Toxic Drugs. Dong Bifu was sentenced to life imprisonment for trafficking in drug pellets. Hu Litang was given a reduced sentence of ten years' imprisonment for helping to sell them. The order was approved by the Nanchang Camp and returned to the county government of this county yesterday for imprisonment.

Young Girl Dies from Abortion 118

Yu Xilin, a resident of Dajia Lane, Yangjiawei, Ninth District of the county, and Chen Zhiyi from Yangxiang, Yanqiao, jointly founded the Shuangli Seed Breeding Farm, which was doing average business. However, Zhiyi had a weakness for women.巧鳳 Qiao Feng, Yu Xilin's niece (20 years old), had some beauty and was awaiting marriage. Chen fell in love at first sight and seduced her. Before long, he had illicit relations with her. After several amorous encounters, she became pregnant. Recently, her belly bulged. Zhiyi then instigated her to go to Chen's house in Yangxiang to have an abortion. Because the medicine was strong, her lower body was injured, causing her extreme pain and moaning. The situation was quite critical. Zhiyi knew that things were bad, so he secretly hired a boat to send Qiao Feng to Yu's house. She died of her ailments at noon the day before yesterday. Qiao Feng's father, Pinshan, learned of the previous events and was furious. He then negotiated with Chen, but it has not yet been resolved.

Jiangyin Chinese and Foreign Ships Allowed to Load and Unload Passengers and Cargo in Cheng 119

The Jiangyin Branch of the Zhenjiang Customs has been ordered to be upgraded to a place for loading and unloading passengers and cargo. Yesterday, Superintendent Jia Guilin and Customs Commissioner Zhang Boli issued a proclamation to Chinese and foreign merchants and various shipping companies. All matters concerning the three marine vessels entering the Yangtze River under the management of the Branch Customs will still be handled in accordance with the regulations, without any changes. The steamships that regularly travel the Yangtze River will be allowed to load and unload passengers and cargo in Jiangyin in accordance with the regulations for places where passengers and cargo are loaded and unloaded. As for the steamships coming from domestic coastal areas and from overseas to China, if they want to sail to Jiangyin for trade, they must first sail to the first treaty port, report to the customs there, and obtain a special permit to sail to the inner port of Jiangyin. They must also list the foreign goods carried in the ship, have them checked by the customs, and pay the taxes there before reporting to the Wusong Branch Customs and obtaining permission to enter the Yangtze River before they can sail to Jiangyin. In the future, when leaving Jiangyin, they must still sail back to the original port in accordance with the regulations for ships sailing in the inner port and return the inner port special permit. If domestic goods are transported from Jiangyin to overseas, they should first report to the branch customs office there. Within the scope that is possible, the branch customs office will send personnel to inspect it. However, the export tax should be paid to the customs office that issued the inner port special permit. If domestic goods are transported from Jiangyin to a treaty port by an inner port steamship, or from a treaty port to Jiangyin, they will be exempt from transit tax. As for sailing to the Wusong Branch Customs, because it is stipulated in the Yangtze River navigation regulations and must be reported to the branch customs, the domestic goods it carries will also not be subject to transit tax.

Nantong Water Police Suppress Bandits in Dongling Port 120

At the end of last month, the 13th Squad of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police sailed from Sanjiazhen and encountered five bandit ships on the waters of Dongling Port in Rugao County. The two sides opened fire. The bandits were unable to withstand the force and fled to the northwest. A four-masted bandit ship was seized, more than a dozen bandits were killed, and a kidnapped person was rescued. The water police squad is still pursuing and suppressing the bandits in the Fenghuan Port area.

Haimen Suffers from Food Shortages and Panic Among the People 121

This county has suffered a long drought this year, and the autumn harvest is less than 40%. The grain reserves in each district have been exhausted in this winter season, resulting in rising market prices. There have been incidents of poor people starving to death from time to time. Yesterday (the 3rd), all the district chiefs held a meeting in the county government, and it was decided that the district chiefs would convene the wealthy people in their respective districts to raise funds to purchase a large amount of grain from other counties for regulation. At the same time, the county government ordered the Food Administration Committee to properly formulate relief measures.

An Assassinated Male Corpse Discovered in Chenjiazhuang, Yangzhou 122

A nameless male corpse was discovered in Chenjiazhuang, Phoenix Bridge, outside the North Gate of this county in the morning of the previous day (3rd). He was about 30 years old. The policeman Wu Zheng Gao discovered the corpse and reported it to the local prosecutor's office for inspection. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Meng led the bailiffs and police officers to the scene and found that the corpse was bald and had no shoes, socks, or belt around his waist. He was only wearing a small lined jacket on his upper body and a single pair of pants on his lower body. His body was covered with wounds. He had died from injuries before his death. However, the cause of death, according to general speculation, was probably that he was killed for adultery. Because Prosecutor Meng could not find any relatives of the deceased, he ordered the policeman to collect the body and ordered the arrest of the murderer.

An Elderly Man in His Seventies Was Rescued After Attempting Suicide 124

Xu Liuer, a native of Shaoxing, is 71 years old this year. Because his hometown was destroyed by fire, everything was reduced to ashes. His son is doing business in Suzhou, so he borrowed three yuan from a friend to come to Hangzhou and then go to Suzhou. Unexpectedly, he lost the money on the way. He could not borrow money in Hangzhou and hanged himself in a toilet on Yanling Road. He was discovered by someone who reported it to the police, who arrived and rescued him. He was barely breathing and was sent to the Public Security Bureau for relief.

Wang Peishi, the county magistrate of Lujiang County, Anhui Province, and Tian Yongnan, the financial committee member, were accused of issuing IOUs without authorization, three times in total, amounting to 45,000 yuan, and forcing residents of the county to share the burden, as well as setting deadlines for payment and ordering the security team of the county to extort money with weapons, occupying and harassing the area. [Local News of This City]

Shanghai Representatives Commemorated the Zhaohe Uprising Yesterday 126

The Municipal Party Headquarters and the Seamen's Party Headquarters

Both Reported the Significance of the Commemoration

Central News Agency reports: At 10 a.m. yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters convened people from all walks of life in the auditorium to hold a memorial meeting for the Zhaohe Uprising. Tong Xingbai, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, presided over the meeting, reported the course of the uprising, and its significance. The meeting then ended with the shouting of slogans. The details are as follows:

Representatives Participating in the Municipal Party Headquarters 127

Chen Xiupu of the Fourth District Silk Reeling Industry Union, Gu Caijiang of the Seventh District Sanitation Industry Union, Gao Jie of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, Wang Longzhang of the Cooperative Enterprise Promotion Association, Yu Zhenhui of the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association, Yu Yuanru of the Sixth District Tea Manufacturing Union, Yu Yaoqiu of the Dry Goods Union, Ma Hanfeng of the Labor Education Committee, Long Peiyun of the General Labor Union, Ren Bin of the Bone and Ivory Utensil Union, Liu Yongkang of the Pharmaceutical Industry Professional Union, He Yuanming of the Accountants' Association, and all staff of the Municipal Party Headquarters, totaling more than 300 people.

Chairman's Report: After performing the ceremony, Chairman Tong Xingbai reported that after the Revolution of 1911, Yuan Shikai monopolized power. Some comrades of our party were induced by profit and fame to seek promotion and fortune, but most still adhered to their revolutionary spirit and did not collude with Yuan. After the Second Revolution, Yuan's massacre of party members became even more intensified. However, the comrades of our party, although unable to gain a foothold in the country, still worked hard overseas to make revolution, taking the opportunity to return home to fight to the death with the counter-revolutionary forces. In 1915, Premier Sun Yat-sen led all revolutionary comrades to plan to overthrow Yuan. Premier Sun then ordered Mr. Chen Qimei to return home to take charge of everything. At that time, Yuan's henchman Zheng Ruicheng led a large army to garrison Shanghai and also controlled the navy. Therefore, Mr. Chen Qimei believed that it would be difficult to launch an uprising unless Zheng was removed. He then sent a comrade to assassinate Zheng at the Baidu Bridge. After Zheng's death, Yuan sent Yang Shanduo to be the Songhu Military Governor. Mr. Chen Qimei then sent Comrade Yang Hu to mobilize the army and navy to launch an uprising. Given the weakness of the revolutionary forces and the difficulty of the economy at the time, the fact that more than 20 people occupied Zhaohe is worthy of admiration. Therefore, although it failed, it was a very glorious event in revolutionary history. We have two feelings when commemorating the Zhaohe Uprising today: (1) The Zhaohe Uprising was to fight to the death with the traitors of the Republic of China created by our party, regardless of all sacrifices and going forward courageously. Therefore, we should still maintain this spirit today to eliminate the traitors who are destroying the Republic of China. These traitors are today's Red bandits. (2) We should unite sincerely and work together to revive China. The comrades at that time, although weak in strength and facing difficult circumstances, loved the Republic of China so much. We should strive today so as not to betray the martyrs.

Commemorative Slogans: (1) The Zhaohe Uprising is the key to the revival of the Republic of China; (2) The Zhaohe Uprising is the prelude to the Yunnan Uprising; (3) Eliminate the Red bandits; (4) Strive for production and construction; (5) Long live the Kuomintang; (6) Long live the Republic of China.

Seamen's Party Headquarters 128

The Special Party Headquarters of the Chinese Seamen held a memorial meeting for the 19th anniversary of the Zhaohe Uprising at 9 a.m. yesterday (the 5th) in the auditorium of the Party Headquarters. All members, staff, and representatives of various seamen's organizations of the Shanghai District Party Headquarters participated. After the ceremony, Secretary Chen Songping, the chairman, reported that the adverse domestic and international political environment of 1915 was first described. The spirit of the martyred martyrs and Mr. Yang Hu, who sacrificed themselves for the party and the country, was admirable. Then, the significance of the Zhaohe Uprising was expounded: one was to eliminate autocracy, revive the Republic of China, and open up the light of China's political history; one was to overthrow Yuan and resist the violent Japanese, crush the legal basis of the Twenty-One Demands, and keep the Chinese flag alive without being cut off. Finally, all the seamen were encouraged to follow the bloody footprints of the martyrs of the Zhaohe Uprising, inherit the pioneering road of the advanced members of the Party, work hard to eliminate the Red bandits, stabilize society, increase production, and relieve the national crisis, so that China can be elevated to the realm of the Three Principles of the People. Then, the seamen's representatives delivered speeches and shouted slogans. The meeting ended at 11 a.m. At the same time, a letter to the seamen was distributed in commemoration of the 19th anniversary of the Zhaohe warship uprising, saying: Dear seamen comrades, the wheels of the times are constantly moving forward. In a flash, the 19th anniversary of the Zhaohe Uprising, which frightened Yuan Shikai to death and revived the Republic of China, has arrived. This revolutionary act, which will be recorded in history, is worthy of our enthusiastic commemoration. After the Revolution of 1911 was completed and Premier Sun Yat-sen took office as President, it was originally hoped that the people would be of one mind, lay out new policies, and seek infinite happiness for the country and the nation. However, at that time, party members with weak wills were either confused by the words of ["the revolutionary army rises, the revolutionary party disappears"] or indulged in the idea of climbing dragons and clinging to phoenixes in order to seize profits and benefits. They betrayed Premier Sun Yat-sen and supported Yuan. This led to the shaking of the revolutionary front of the Party, and the great plan of national construction could not be realized. Premier Sun Yat-sen always held the spirit of ["Better to be a broken jade than a whole tile"]. Seeing this situation, he resigned. The power then fell into the hands of Yuan. Yuan was a treacherous and evil villain with different ambitions. Once he monopolized power, he excluded dissidents, widely planted minions, and hoped to realize his dream of becoming an emperor. He then proceeded to borrow heavily from the five countries, bribing members and spies, destroying the Provisional Constitution, colluding with Japan, and even frantically recognizing the Twenty-One Demands that would destroy the country, causing the lifeline of the country to be on the verge of collapse. At that time, Premier Sun Yat-sen was in Japan. Upon hearing the news, he was filled with grief and anger. He deeply knew that the work of overthrowing Yuan and protecting the country could no longer be delayed. Therefore, he sent comrades such as Ju Zheng and Zhu Zhixin to Shandong, Guangdong, and other places to carry out activities. At the same time, he believed that Shanghai was the throat of the Yangtze River and the hub of the north and south. If it could be occupied, Jiangbiao would certainly fall at the mere sight of it. Therefore, he sent Chen Qimei, Yang Hu, and other comrades to take charge of the work in Shanghai. Yuan also realized the agitation of the Party against the imperial system and was eager to find ways to defend it. He was especially afraid of the activists led by Chen Qimei and others. Therefore, he sent his capable henchman Zheng Ruicheng to garrison Shanghai with a large army and strictly guarded it. Comrade Chen Qimei knew that Shanghai would not be easily launched unless Zheng was removed. Therefore, he sent comrades Wang Mingshan and Wang Xiaofeng, who were proficient in shooting, to kill him on the side of the Baidu Bridge. After Zheng Ruicheng, whom Yuan relied on as the Great Wall, died, Comrade Chen Qimei took advantage of the popular sentiment and the unsettled deployment of Yuan to send Comrade Yang Hu on December 5 to lead a death squad to seize the Zhaohe warship and formally launch a campaign against Yuan. Comrade Yang Hu also announced the Party's aims and the purpose of the Yuan campaign to the Marine Corps. All were happy to accept command and fired cannons at the Yuan army in the arsenal. Comrades on the shore responded one after another and successively occupied important institutions such as the telegraph bureau. Ultimately, due to the disparity in numbers and the disparity in weapons, the land route failed one after another. The Zhaohe warship was also attacked by the rebel parties Yingrui and Tongji, making it difficult to defend. Comrade Yang Hu and others had no choice but to disguise themselves and swim away. The wounded comrades in the ship were all captured and killed by Yuan's army. This loud and thunderous event that shocked China and foreign countries unfortunately ended in failure. Considering that the Zhaohe Uprising, although unsuccessful, at a time when Yuan's imperial dream was in full swing and a group of shameless people were petitioning for and urging him to advance, our revolutionary soldiers were able to assassinate Yuan's brave general and seize warships from heavy military pressure and strict logic, thus promoting the revolutionary forces lurking in various provinces to rise one after another. The cannon of Zhaohe can be described as the prelude to the destruction of the imperial system and the alarm bell to awaken the national soul. Dear seamen comrades, the grand event of the Zhaohe Uprising has been recorded in the history books and will be immortalized forever. The families of the martyrs of the Zhaohe Uprising have also been given preferential treatment by the central government by Comrade Yang Hu, who also founded Zhaohe Middle School, which widely accepts the children of the martyrs, so that their education is well-suited. The martyrs of Zhaohe have removed their burdens and can close their eyes in the afterlife. However, looking back at the universe, thorns and copper camels, the national crisis is imminent, and it is time for us to devote our lives to serve the country. Now, please raise two matters as common goals for our efforts: 1. Assist the government in eliminating the Red bandits and stabilizing society; 2. Work hard in our positions, increase production, and enrich national power. The storm is dark, but the cock is still crowing. I hope that my seamen comrades will work together to make it happen. Slogans: 1. The Zhaohe Uprising was a revolutionary feat to overthrow the imperial system and safeguard the Republic of China; 2. The Zhaohe Uprising was a major key to the revival of the Republic of China; 3. The Zhaohe Uprising was a successful prelude to the Yunnan Uprising; 4. The Zhaohe Uprising was a struggle between democratic forces and the remnants of autocracy; 5. To commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising, we must eliminate the Red bandits and stabilize society; 6. To commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising, we must strive for construction and enrich national power; 7. Inherit the revolutionary spirit of the Zhaohe Uprising predecessors to resist foreign aggression; 8. Long live the Kuomintang; 9. Long live the Republic of China. Propaganda Section of the Special Party Headquarters of the Chinese Seamen, December.

League of Nations Experts Departed for Beijing and Hangzhou Separately Yesterday 133

Kothari Left for Hangzhou Yesterday Morning for Inspection

Voumot Left by Train for Beijing Last Night

Mr. Kothari and Mr. Voumot, the League of Nations technical experts who came to China upon invitation, paid a visit to Mr. Song Ziwen, the standing committee member of the National Economic Council, immediately after arriving in Shanghai on the 4th. Mr. Kothari then, at 10:00 AM yesterday morning, accompanied by Kang Shizhen, the technician of the Highway Department of the National Economic Council, and Consultant Pu, took a car and followed the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway to Hangzhou to inspect the road. After arriving in Hangzhou, they will go to various highways in Zhejiang for a week of inspection, and then enter Beijing along the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway. As for Mr. Voumot, he was accompanied by Guo Dehua, the secretary specially sent by the Economic Council to Shanghai to welcome the two experts, and took a night express train to Beijing at around 11:00 PM last night. It is scheduled to stay in Beijing for a few days. After Kothari arrives in Beijing from Zhejiang, they will go to the Northwest together for inspection.

Finland's Independence Day Today 135

Finnish Nationals Hold Celebrations

Consulate General Broadcasts Special Programs

Today is the 17th anniversary of the declaration of independence of the Republic of Finland. Finnish nationals in this city will hold celebrations. According to reports, the President of Finland, Svinhufvud, was born in 1861 and comes from a prominent family. After graduating from the Faculty of Law of the University of Helsinki in 1886, he practiced law. Later, he organized a passive resistance movement with Finnish patriots to resist the Great Slavism in order to preserve Finland's internal independence. Although Finland had its own government, parliament, administrative organs, currency, and independent economic life at that time, it was under the rule of the Russian Emperor. Since 1809, when Finland broke away from Sweden due to war, successive Russian Emperors have sworn to abide by Finland's independent economic life. In 1809, the Russian authorities began to try to assimilate Finland into Russia, but the effect was to greatly damage the relationship between the two peoples and gain nothing. In 1905, Finland changed to a unicameral system. Two years later, Svinhufvud was elected as a member of parliament and served as the speaker of the parliament for several terms, taking great care to protect the happiness of the Finnish people. At the beginning of the European War, Russia's oppression of Finland became even more severe. Svinhufvud, then a judge of the local court, resisted the illegal orders of the Russian government and was arrested in November 1914 and exiled to a remote village in Tomsk, Siberia. A recent photo of the Finnish President, 1917.

In March of that year, the Finnish Revolution occurred, and Svinhufvud was able to return to his country and was warmly welcomed by the people. He was immediately appointed as the Minister of Justice. From the autumn of that year to January of 1891, he served as Prime Minister. On December 4, 1917, Svinhufvud, in his capacity as Prime Minister, delivered the government's resolution on Finland's independence at the plenary session of the Finnish Parliament. Two days later, it was formally announced by the Parliament. From January 1918 to the summer of 1930, Svinhufvud retired to the countryside, devoting himself to social undertakings and achieving much. He then returned to serve as Prime Minister until March 1931, when he was elected as the President of Finland. Since taking office, he has worked hard to govern the country, and the country's strength has been increasing, so he is greatly loved by the people. Although Svinhufvud is already 73 years old, he is physically strong and mentally vigorous. He is good at shooting and enjoys hunting. Last year, he won the national shooting competition for seniors. The people often call him "Old Peter" or "Finland's Elder Statesman," which shows their feelings for the founding father of the country.

The Finnish Consulate General in this city will take the 6th of this month as the 17th anniversary of Finland's independence and will specially broadcast a special program at the Duncun Radio Station on Minguo Road in this city from 7:45 PM to 8:30 PM. First, the consulate will introduce the Republic of Finland, briefly describing the country's recent situation, and then continue to broadcast Finnish records. Finnish music is world-famous, especially Finnish marches, which are majestic and moving and popular. Wireless radio listeners in this city can have a feast for their ears at that time.

Page 11

Zhu Pu Returns from Study Tour 142

Discusses Danish Agricultural Cooperation

Zhu Pu, a counselor of the Executive Yuan and specialist of the Rural Rehabilitation Committee, was ordered this summer to go to Europe and the United States to study agricultural cooperation. He returned to Shanghai on the Empress of Canada yesterday (the 5th). A reporter from the New Voice News Agency met him on the ship and asked about the results of his trip. He answered as follows:

Studied in More Than Ten Countries 143

Zhu said, "I went abroad in early June of this year and it has been half a year now. During these six months, I have studied in more than ten countries, including Italy, Switzerland, France, Belgium, England, Holland, Germany, Denmark, Sweden, Canada, and the United States. The time spent in Denmark was the longest, almost three months. Because Denmark is known as a cooperative country, its agricultural cooperation is particularly developed. Therefore, when I went abroad, I focused on Denmark as my target. The results of the study were very satisfactory. India and Japan also have considerable achievements in agricultural cooperation. Unfortunately, I passed by in a hurry and did not have the opportunity to visit them, which I regret. Regarding the situation of Danish agricultural cooperation, it cannot be fully described in a short time. I will briefly talk about its general situation to inform the people of the country."

Danish Agricultural Cooperation 144

Denmark is a small country, with an area of only 16,576 square miles, which is less than half of Zhejiang, the smallest province in our country. Its population is only 3,550,656 people, which is less than half of Gansu, the smallest province in our country. But its agricultural abundance, social stability, and people's happiness are unmatched by any country in the world. The reason for this is entirely due to the success of the cooperative movement. The Danish people, nineteen, are members of the cooperative society. The history of the cooperative movement in Denmark is not very long. Seventy years ago, the situation in Denmark was no different from that in our country today. At that time, Denmark had just failed in the war against Prussia and Austria in 1864 and suffered extremely severe natural disasters. As a result, the decline of industry and the economic panic reached their peak. The Danish people, seeing the dangerous situation, tried to save themselves and followed the example of England in promoting the cooperative movement. It has only been a few decades since then.

Socialization of Distribution 145

"The most proud phenomenon of Denmark today is what Mr. Sun Yat-sen said: 'Socialization of distribution. The people of the whole country have neither the so-called rich nor the poor. Everyone is well-fed and clothed and happy. This has realized the ideal of cooperativism. At the same time, it is enough to show that this phenomenon cannot be achieved by capitalist countries or communist countries.' Denmark's agricultural products, pickled meat, eggs, and butter are the three major items. The countries with the widest sales are England and Germany. Ninety-nine percent of the pickled meat is sold to England, and only one percent is used by the country itself. Eighty-five percent of the eggs are sold to England, fourteen percent are sold to Germany, and only one percent is used by the country itself. Sixty-eight percent of the butter is sold to England, twenty-five percent is sold to Germany, and only seven percent is used by the country itself. Such things are too numerous to mention. In recent years, due to the general decline in the economic situation of various countries in the world, England has imposed a so-called quota system on Denmark's imported goods. Germany is on the verge of bankruptcy due to economic and financial difficulties and has no ability to buy foreign goods. Therefore, Denmark has been quite affected."

No Sign of Recession 146

"But according to my observation in various villages in Denmark, its prosperous image is still enviable everywhere and is by no means as fully expressed as the recession that can be seen at a glance in other countries. The economic foundation of the Danish countryside is extremely solid, and it is not enough to frustrate its slightest bit by being slightly affected by foreign countries for a while. After observing Denmark, I felt that agricultural cooperation should be promoted more in our country. At present, all parties in the government and the public have paid considerable attention to and promoted this, but it is hoped that the people of the country will rise up together and regard it as the only way to revitalize the countryside. The future of agriculture and people's livelihood in our country will rely on it."

Still Going Abroad for Study Tour 147

It is reported that Zhu feels slightly unwell due to the hardship of the journey and plans to rest in Shanghai for one or two days before going to Beijing to visit President Wang and report everything. It is also reported that Zhu has temporarily requested leave to return to the country for personal matters this time and will soon go to other countries for a long-term study tour and research to continue the unfinished mission.

When passing through Wuxi, they visited major factories. Yesterday they finished their sightseeing and came to Shanghai and stayed at the New Asia and Huizhong hotels. Upon arrival, they visited Liang Xinji's Liang Bozhi and asked him to introduce them to various factories in Shanghai. Then Liang Bozhi, together with Huang Hanliang of Guanshengyuan Food Factory, led them to visit various factories. After visiting Liang Xinji and Guanshengyuan factories in the morning of the 4th, they had lunch. Huang Hanliang hosted a banquet at the Guanshengyuan Farm in Caohejing. The Contract for the Anhui Province's 1.2 Million Loan is About to be Signed 151

800,000 Yuan to be Released First on the 15th of this Month

Monthly Interest of 8% to Begin in February Next Year

Xinxin News Agency reports: The Anhui Provincial Government, due to the severity of this year's famine and the sharp reduction in tax revenues, is experiencing difficulties in administrative expenses. Mao Longzhang, the Director of the Finance Department, came to Shanghai to contact the Central, China, Jiaotong, Shanghai, and China Industrial Banks. It was decided to borrow 1.2 million yuan at a monthly interest rate of 8%. The repayment will begin in February next year and will be repaid in full in 20 months. The draft loan contract was signed in Shanghai on the 24th of last month. Director Mao took it back to Anhui Province and reported it to the provincial government. It will be officially signed in Wuhu. A reporter from Xinxin News Agency learned from the borrowing bank yesterday morning that the formal loan contract for Anhui Province has been sent from Shanghai to Wuhu. The Finance Department of the province has sent Li Shiqian to Wuhu to be responsible for contacting the branches of the lending banks. It can be officially signed within days. As for the release of funds, it was originally stipulated that 800,000 yuan would be released on December 1, 200,000 yuan would be released on February 1 next year, and 200,000 yuan would be released on June 1. Since the formal contract could not be signed as scheduled before December 1, the first installment, which was scheduled to be released on December 1, has now been decided to be changed to December 15, when the Wuhu branches of the lending banks will release 800,000 yuan to the Anhui Provincial Government. The remaining 400,000 yuan will still be released on the originally scheduled date.

The details are as follows:

Taishan Ship: After it was confirmed that it had sunk, all 45 crew members were killed. Xingshi Ship: The total tonnage is 2,018 tons. This time, it loaded salt from Haizhou and sailed to Hankou. It ran aground on the Datong River. It has been towed by the Songpu ship and reported to Shanghai yesterday that it has been rescued and is undamaged and is sailing to Hankou as usual.

Jianghai Customs Flag Station Change of Wind Signal 153

Effective January 1st of next year

The Jianghai Customs Port Affairs Department, in order to have the customs flag station change to wind signal, specially issued a notice yesterday, which stated: [It has been decided that starting January 1st, 1935 of the Republic of China, the black signal for indicating approaching hurricanes or strong winds will be changed to two black balls hanging vertically in a string. From this day forward, all wind signal indicators of this customs will be displayed at three locations: the flag station on the customs rooftop, and the top poles of the Peace Dock water tower, as follows: ㈠ When predicting a drastic change in weather, one black ball will be hung during the day, and one red light will be hung at night. ㈡ When predicting a gale or strong wind, two black balls will be hung vertically in a string during the day, and two red lights will be hung side by side at night. At the same time, a cannon will be fired once from the flag stations at Lujiazui and Lan Road in Pudong. This signal is only to supplement the insufficient extraordinary wind signals on the Chinese sea surface shown by the Xujiahui Observatory signal tower in the French Concession, and to warn small boats in this port. It is hereby notified to all shipping merchants for their information. Signed, Port Director Gullion.]

Jisheng Society's Investigation Report on Zhejiang Disaster 157

The Chinese Jisheng Society previously dispatched personnel to Zhejiang, Shanghai, and Ningbo for emergency relief. According to the investigation report, the devastation in the disaster area is unbearable to witness and difficult to describe in detail. According to the society's investigation, in the 353rd district, the initial report stated that there were 17,800 disaster-stricken households in the 9th district, with approximately 5 or 6 people per household. The first report stated that there were more than 8,380 disaster-stricken households in the 3 districts, also with 5 or 6 people per household. The number of households in the district that has just been investigated, according to local reports, is approximately 11,000, and the number of people per household is the same as before. This district is still under review and has not yet been completed. The society believes that the relief funds are limited and insufficient to handle the situation alone, so it is jointly managed with the Shanghai Foreign Relief Association, the Shanghai Relief Association, and the Hai Ning local relief associations. In terms of the number of households to be restored, the amount received per person is very small. It is not yet time to consider winter plowing and saving lives. Other areas, such as Haiyan, which have suffered disasters, are also planning to distribute emergency relief. The society is unable to support this on its own, and the funds for joint management have not yet been collected, making it difficult to start. Furthermore, many counties in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces have suffered severe disasters. Representatives reported that their tears had run dry in Shanghai. The society is currently unable to proceed. Although the number of relief funds received is decreasing due to the sluggish market, fellow philanthropists at home and abroad should, in this time of extraordinary disaster, make vows to provide relief. The merit is ten times greater than usual. Saving one person's life is better than building a seven-story pagoda. The more people you save, the greater the merit and the immeasurable blessings. Moreover, it is now winter, and hunger and cold are biting. The lives of half of the disaster victims who have not yet died are hanging by a thread, and their suffering is indescribable.

Petitioning in Beijing The association dispatched Chairman Chu Huiseng on the Shanghai-Beijing train at 4 PM yesterday to petition party and state leaders such as Bu Lei, Zhou Chenqin, and Dai Jitao, requesting the central government to allocate winter relief funds to Zhejiang province.

News from the Jiangsu Provincial Small-Capital Loan Office for Common People 160

Jiangsu Provincial Chairman Guo Bufei and Finance Director Zhao Dihua are concerned about helping the common people of this province who are engaged in small-scale businesses. They have previously proposed establishing a small-capital loan office, which will be jointly operated by Jin Cheng, Farmers, and Jiangsu banks. Yesterday, a meeting was held at the Shanghai Jin Cheng Bank. Wu Yunzhai, manager of Shanghai Jin Cheng Bank, Hou Houpei, deputy manager of Farmers Bank, and Tian Shitai, assistant manager of Jiangsu Bank, were appointed as directors of the board. Yang Zhaoxiong and Chen Qiwei, commissioned by the Finance Department, were appointed as supervisors. The loan regulations and operating guidelines were also passed. Hou Houpei was elected as the managing director. The loan rules limit the use of the funds and are divided into four categories: ㈠ Wholesale purchase of goods or raw materials ㈡ Purchase of handicraft and agricultural tools, advance payments for promoting national goods, ㈣ Other productive uses. Any small-scale farmers and merchants with a fixed address and a legitimate business can apply for a loan. The general office is located at the Zhenjiang Farmers Bank, and the first branch office is at the Jiangsu Bank outside Zhenjiang. It is expected to be established and begin lending soon. The loan amount ranges from one yuan to a maximum of one hundred yuan. In the future, small-scale common people will undoubtedly benefit greatly. It is said that the director and deputy director of the office have also been internally decided and will be announced soon.

Notice Regarding Mailing New Year's Cards 164

Must Be Bundled Separately When Mailing

According to the Shanghai Postal Authority, as the end of the year approaches, the New Year's cards and other mail received and sent by the post office will inevitably become crowded day by day. If senders can bundle the three types of items—those sent to this port, domestic, and foreign—separately and then mail them, delivery will definitely be extra fast. Also, if you have invitations to be sent, it is best to bundle them separately and not mix them with New Year's cards to avoid delays.

As for letters sent from Shen (Shanghai), they can also be sealed directly to Shanghai using the post office box, which is more convenient and reliable than entrusting boats and ship personnel for forwarding. It is also reported that the post office box handles registered mail, so there is no loss of mail. There are quite a few people from that area living in Shanghai, which should be very convenient.

Health Bureau Investigates the Cause of Food Poisoning 170

Confirmed That the Tragedy Was Caused by Cooking and Selling Pufferfish

On November 28th, a food poisoning incident occurred at the Xieshunxing restaurant on Oujia Road in Zhabei, resulting in the death of as many as eleven diners. There were various rumors about the cause of the poisoning. The Municipal Health Bureau dispatched personnel to investigate the matter thoroughly on the 29th and determined that it was caused by cooking and selling pufferfish that poisoned the diners. The following is the Health Bureau's handling of this case: The Health Bureau dispatched Cheng Shuzhen, the director of the Health Experiment Institute, Wu Liguo, the chief of the Third Section, and Jiang Shicheng, a technician, to investigate. Director Cheng and others first went to the Linping Road Police Station, which has jurisdiction over the area, and were received by Police Officer Chen. They also questioned the shop employees who were in custody. According to them, the shop had purchased over a hundred catties of fish with black backs and white bellies, about half a foot long, four days ago. They cooked a pot every day and sold it to diners by the bowl. At 2 PM yesterday, two customers came to the shop and questioned why they felt numb and heavy-headed after eating the fish. Unexpectedly, two hours later, the two died in the shop one after another. When asked what kind of fish they had purchased and cooked, they claimed that it was indeed pufferfish and that they dared not lie. They then went to inspect the Xieshunxing restaurant, where they saw that the door was closed and a police officer was guarding it. Inside, they saw two corpses with no special phenomena. They did not find any remaining fish, only fish bones and shredded fish meat in the rice bucket. There seemed to be vomit on the ground, but it had been swept away. They then visited the Tongren Hospital, where they were received by Dr. Huang Mingxin. According to him, five poisoned patients were sent in succession on the afternoon of the 28th. One person died before arriving at the hospital, and two others were completely paralyzed, had difficulty breathing, and had dilated pupils with no spasms. Artificial respiration was used, but soon their breathing stopped, although their hearts were still active. Finally, they died. Another patient had almost recovered and was not in danger. When asked what they had eaten, they said they had only eaten a bowl of fish and rice and had not drunk alcohol. Unexpectedly, an hour after eating, their lips and fingers first became numb, followed by their whole body. They felt heavy-headed and short of breath and knew that something was wrong. They quickly used their hands to induce vomiting a total of five times. After being admitted to the hospital, they gradually recovered. Based on the results of the investigation, it was determined that it was pufferfish poisoning. It was also reported that the pufferfish in the shop had been purchased from the 16th Pier. The Health Bureau has notified the French Concession Public Works Bureau to strictly ban this practice. As for the medical treatment after poisoning, in addition to injecting cardiac stimulants and using artificial respiration, injecting adrenaline and pituitary extract can be effective.

Lu Plans to Sell Private Property to Repay Debts

Xu First Trialed the Criminal Case and Then Retried the Civil Case

After the China Industrial Bank closed down, Lu Xihou, its managing director, and Lu Mengxiang, who took over as manager after the fleeing manager Qin Baoyuan, and Sun Xiren, the manager of the Shenghua Trading Company set up by Qin Baoyuan, were found by the police to have colluded in fraud. They were all additionally prosecuted together. The court has repeatedly summoned them for trial, but not all defendants have appeared in court. The details have been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Criminal Judge Hong Yeye conducted another trial. Many creditors, concerned about their interests, still

Attended the Hearing 172

The lawyer for the police prosecutor, Ru Baobi, stated that regarding the China Industrial Bank's mortgaging of title deeds to the Si Ming Bank, the judge had personally gone to Si Ming on the 29th of last month to investigate the relevant accounts, and a report has already been submitted for review. Judge Qian then instructed Lu Xihou, stating that the China Industrial Bank used four title deeds as collateral to obtain treasury bonds from the Si Ming Bank on October 25th of last year. The total amount of treasury bonds obtained was 270,000. These title deeds were originally mortgaged by your wife, Wang Guozhi, to the savings department of the China Industrial Bank on October 24th for a consideration of 70,000 yuan. According to your confession, the collateral must be transferred to another account. However, this court investigated the Thales Yanghang and Aierde Yanghang, where the title deeds were registered, and found that one deed from Thales was transferred on the 21st of the month,

To Si Ming's Account 173

And three deeds from Aierde were transferred to Si Ming's account on October 23rd. The dates are all before the date you stated that Wang Guozhi mortgaged them to the China Industrial Bank. Even if it is not a case of one deed being used twice, in any case, the mortgage to the China Industrial Bank must be nominal. Lu, upon hearing this instruction, confessed that the title deeds were originally taken from his wife and then transferred to Si Ming. However, he previously stated that his memory of the date was unclear. The judge then asked the defendant Sun Xiren, "Qin Baoyuan previously confessed at the police station that after the China Industrial Bank went bankrupt, you still often went to the bank to hold meetings. What did you discuss?" Sun completely denied this. Lu Mengxiang said that he had seen Sun go to the bank once, but he had not heard about the buying and selling of rayon. The savings department owes more than 560,000 yuan. This court has appointed another judge to handle the liquidation matters. How will you handle the aftermath? owing as much as 600,000. Despite repeated demands, and informing him that this amount was related to the guarantee for savings depositors, not a single penny had been repaid. Old Mrs. Yu, Kidnapped, Falls Ill from Fright 177

Injured Kidnapper Also Not Yet Healed

Case Adjourned for Trial Next Week

Old Mrs. Yu, a Cantonese resident at No. 64, Avenue Amiral de Gueydon in the French Concession, was kidnapped around 8 a.m. on October 21st while taking a chartered car to the cathedral for mass. The kidnapping occurred near the intersection of the Jiangsu Higher Court, Jiangsu First Branch Court, and Jiangsu Second Branch Court, not far from her home. The kidnappers sent a letter to her family demanding a ransom of 100,000 yuan. It was not until the 19th of last month that the Jiangning Police Station learned that Ziying and Zhou Bingcheng, etc. were at the Sanxin Inn outside the Chang Gate in Suzhou posing as representatives sent by the victim to negotiate the ransom. Two kidnappers from Shaoxing, Li Xiaoxiao, and Wang Fukang from Huzhou were apprehended. After interrogation, they revealed that the hostage was being held in a room at No. 186 Jianlin Road, Hongkou, Shanghai. The French Concession police were immediately notified by long-distance telephone and dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives, along with additional Chinese and foreign detectives from the Yulin Road Police Station, to rescue the hostage and arrest Hui Zhi, the guard, and Zhou Juqin, a woman. At the time, the kidnappers opened fire to resist the detectives, who returned fire. Two kidnappers, Lin De and Tao Shuigen, were wounded. Simultaneously, detective Zhang Chunsheng from the police station was also shot and wounded. All were sent to the Guangci Hospital. Meanwhile, detectives Zhang and Zhou transported the two kidnappers, Li and Wang, from Suzhou to Shanghai, where they were handed over to the First Special Court for detention and investigation. The injured kidnapper Tao Shuigen died from his wounds after ineffective treatment. The death was reported to the court for verification, and the body was collected by a charitable organization for burial. The details have been previously reported. The police have now completed their investigation into the case. Yesterday, Judge Xiong Huiping, accompanied by clerk Tao Zongkan, specially convened the criminal court for a trial. According to the police lawyer Yao Zhaodi, the victim, Mrs. Yu, has been ill in hospital since the incident due to fright and has not yet recovered. The injured kidnapper has also not yet healed. Therefore, a special request was made for a further adjournment for trial next week. The court approved the request and adjourned the trial to February 11th. The defendants remain in custody.
