Petition from the Bihan Shelter for Vacating the Chao Hui Mountain Villa 183

The poor have nowhere to go and suffer greatly

The Shanghai South Bihan Shelter of the Charitable Organizations Federation yesterday submitted a document to the Social Affairs Bureau stating, "[Respectfully submitted, this association has been running the Bihan Shelter since 1927, and a second branch was established in the Chao Hui Mountain Villa. The buildings in the mountain villa are relatively large and can accommodate a larger number of people. Over the years, the shelter set up in the mountain villa has accommodated more than 3,000 people. This year, due to the stationing of over 100 security team members in the mountain villa, the second Bihan Shelter cannot be opened. There are no suitable places in the Nanshi area to accommodate people. This year, due to rural bankruptcy and industrial and commercial decline, the general population of poor people and unemployed workers is even larger than in previous years. Although the Bihan Shelter has already started accepting people at the Chaozhou Guildhall on the first of this month, it has reached over 500 people in a few days, and poor people continue to arrive in droves, in a miserable and distressing state. It is difficult to find an official place to put them, so we hereby submit this letter to your bureau, requesting that you forward it to the municipal government, asking them to consider the plight of the poor and order the security department to quickly find a way to temporarily move the stationed troops in the mountain villa. The shelter can be returned when the Bihan Shelter finishes its work next spring. This matter concerns relief, so we earnestly request that you promptly review and reply. This is submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau.]" It is heard that the shelter is urgently seeking to expand its location, and it is expected that the authorities will provide assistance to maximize relief efforts. The internal staff of the shelter includes General Manager Zhang Zixin, Accountant Tan Qiutian, General Affairs Chen Yousheng, Document Clerk Wang Shuliu, Clothing Manager Zheng Jingyan, Xu Nianchun, Registration Wang Jueyu, Zhao Jinshen, Reception Kong Xianzhang, Inspection Zhu Boying, and Managers Xu Tianxi, Lu Jiqing, and Mao Jianqing, etc.

Large Quantity of Red Pills Confiscated at South Railway Station 184

217,000 Red Pills Abandoned

Traffickers Abandoned Pills and Fled

At around 5:50 a.m. yesterday at the Shanghai South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, while it was still dark, gold-wearing guard Jin Zhongfu of the Chenjiaqiao Police Station of the Ximen Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau was changing shifts at the front gate of the station. Suddenly, a rickshaw coming from the east carrying a large wooden box, a large rattan black lacquered box, a medium-sized leather suitcase, and a net basket, and one passenger wearing a black robe and a cotton hat with tied threads, about thirty years old and speaking in the local dialect, arrived. As the passenger and the boxes and baskets on the rickshaw got off at the station, guard Jin Zhongfu, who was switching positions with Officer Hu Zhao (the official inspectors had not yet arrived at the station), saw the passenger carrying three large boxes at such an early hour, which seemed suspicious. Therefore, he asked the passenger to open them for inspection. The passenger falsely claimed that the key was with the owner in the back and that he would come right away. At that moment, two other rickshaws arrived, carrying two passengers and luggage. The guard was busy inspecting them and missed the opportunity to prevent the first passenger from abandoning two of the boxes and fleeing without a trace. The guard waited until about 7:00 a.m. without seeing anyone come to claim them, concluding that there was likely a trick involved. He immediately reported to Patrol Leader Hu of the Chenjiaqiao Police Station, who forwarded it to Patrol Inspector Su of the Gaochangmiao Substation and requested instructions. Patrol Inspector Su immediately reported to Director Li of the Ximen Branch by telephone. Director Li personally drove to the South Railway Station and brought the three abandoned boxes and the net basket to the Gaochangmiao Substation for inspection. The large wooden box was filled with eight large packages wrapped in Shen Bao newspaper, which, when opened, were found to contain red pills. Another six large packages were found in the large rattan black lacquered box. Further inspection of the medium-sized leather suitcase also revealed six large packages, making a total of 20 large packages, or 217 bags, each containing approximately 1,000 pills, totaling 217,000 red pills. The prohibited boxes and the net basket were taken to the Ximen Branch and sent to the main bureau for verification. Officers were dispatched to investigate the traffickers and other accomplices and to bring them to justice.

Stepmother Sues Son and Daughter-in-Law Case 185

Judge's Efforts to Mediate Reconciliation Prove Futile

Result: Housemaid Assaulted, Fines Imposed

Zui Shi, the stepmother of Xie Guozhen and Xie Zhou, filed a lawsuit with the Huishi Police against them, and Zhu Zhou, Zhou's sister, and her husband Zhu Songzhou, for jointly injuring her and assaulting the housemaid Hongmei. The case was brought to the First Special Court. Details of the trial have been reported. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhan Liangce of the First Special Court continued the trial in the Fifth Criminal Court. The defendants' lawyers, Zou Yu and Liu Shifang, stated that after ten adjournments, the manager of the American Zui Shi Foreign Company, Mr. Kauff, had intervened to mediate the plaintiff's request for the return of 1,000 yuan in marriage expenses and was still in discussions, requesting an adjournment. However, the plaintiff's lawyer, Yi Yiping, denied any reconciliation. Judge Zhan stated that the case was a family dispute between a mother and son and should not be litigated. The result of litigation would inevitably further damage the relationship between the parties. He urged reconciliation. However, Xie Zheng and Xie Yibin insisted on resolving the matter according to the law. Xie Guozhen stated that although he had not beaten his stepmother, he would be willing to compensate his stepmother for the sake of ending the lawsuit and maintaining family harmony. However, the plaintiff firmly refused. Judge Zhan's attempts at reconciliation were unsuccessful, and he proceeded with the trial. The plaintiff's incidental civil suit requested 50 yuan in medical expenses. The testimony was largely the same as the previous time (reported in this newspaper on the 29th of last month, omitted for brevity). After the police lawyer Jiang Zhilian and the lawyers for the plaintiff and defendants debated each other, Judge Zhan announced the judgment in court: Xie Guozhen and Zhu Songzhou were each fined 50 yuan for bodily harm, with a two-year suspended sentence. Xie Zhou and Zhu Zhou were found not guilty. The plaintiff's incidental civil suit was dismissed. Police lawyer Jiang requested that the defendants be required to post bail during the appeal period. The court then ordered the four defendants to post 100 yuan in cash or a shop guarantee each during the appeal period. Xie and Zhu were convicted of assaulting the housemaid Hongmei, while Zheng was not convicted because the evidence against her was insufficient.

Russian Vendetta Case 187

First Kills Friend's Wife

Then Commits Suicide Out of Fear of Punishment

Russian Belia Lachuck, also known as Simon (transliteration), 40 years old this year, had no occupation or address in Shanghai. Recently, he had a feud with Yevgenia Ivanovskaya (transliteration, 26 years old), the wife of his compatriot Yefim Ivanovsky (transliteration, 30 years old), who lived in Room 8 of Company House No. 10, Lane 9, Avenue Joffre in the French Concession (one theory is that he was jealous due to unrequited love). He planned to kill the woman. At around 3:00 p.m. on the 4th, he hid a knife and rushed to the woman's house. Catching her off guard, he suddenly stabbed the woman in a vital area, killing her instantly. Seeing that his goal had been achieved, the murderer suddenly committed suicide out of fear of punishment. He stabbed himself in the head and neck, pushed open the window, and jumped down, suffering internal and external injuries, dying on the spot. The French police were informed and sent detectives to investigate. They transported the bodies of the man and woman to the autopsy room attached to the Shanghai Municipal Council Hospital on Route Tenant de la Tour. Yesterday morning, prosecutor Wang Ren of the Second Special Court dispatched an investigator, a forensic doctor, and a clerk to the hospital to examine the two bodies. After questioning Ivanovsky, the woman's husband, he instructed that Ivanovskaya's death was caused by knife wounds, and the body was handed over to Ivanovsky for burial. He also instructed that Belia Lachuck's death was caused by suicide, and the body was handed over to the Shanghai Municipal Council for burial.

The Shanghai Evening Post and Mercury reported that Russian Bai Sichuzhi, 36 years old, residing at No. 3, Hehe Lane, Avenue Joffre, yesterday severed the throat of Russian Ivanovska's wife, 25 years old, with a razor due to jealousy. Bai committed suicide by cutting his throat and jumping out of a window from an upper floor. The Second Special District Court examined the two bodies this morning. The incident occurred at 3:30 p.m. yesterday. Ivanovska had left home only minutes before. Ivanovska did not return home until 7:00 p.m., when he learned of his wife's murder. After Ivanovska left home, the murderer, Bai, rushed to the second floor, where the Ivanovska couple lived. Soon, a dispute was heard between Bai and Mrs. Ivanovskaya. Bai and Mrs. Ivanovskaya had been in love for a long time, as everyone knew. Bai had tried to persuade the woman to abandon her husband and run away with him, but had failed. When a housemate went to check because of the loud noise, she found Mrs. Ivanovskaya dead in a pool of blood. She had been killed by Bai with a long razor that cut her throat. Bai fell to the ground below. By the time the police arrived, Bai was dying. Bai had worked at the cafe opened by Ivanovska in Qingdao this summer. Ivanovska had recently been employed by a brewery on Broadway Road. However, both were currently unemployed. Mrs. Ivanovskaya came to Shanghai from Harbin five years ago and married Ivanovska. Her parents and a younger brother and sister still live in Harbin.

American Boxer Sues Dance Hall Manager 188

Assaulted by Musician in Dance Hall, Sues for Damages

Feng Yixiang, 43 years old, from Nantong, and Dong Yunlong, 40 years old, both locals, jointly invested in the Dongfeng Company at No. 9, Avenue Edward VII, opening the Dahua and Dahu dance halls. They also opened a dance hall in the Yiyuan Garden on Rue Amiral Courbet, which was very successful. They hired a Westerner, Entro (transliteration), as manager. Recently, American boxer Riley (transliteration), residing at Apartment 11, No. 96 Boulevard des deux Republiques in the Public Concession, has hired lawyer Fan Kelin to file a lawsuit in the Civil Court of the Second Special District against Feng Yixiang and Dong Yunlong, seeking damages of 5,000 US dollars (approximately 15,000 yuan in national currency) for injuries sustained in an assault by a black musician at the dance hall. According to the plaintiff's statement of claim, he often went to the Yiyuan dance hall during his leisure time. On the evening of the 12th of last month, he was suddenly assaulted by twelve black musicians employed by the dance hall, causing him to be covered in injuries. The defendants, as employers of the dance hall musicians, failed to take preventive measures beforehand and did not stop them afterward, causing the plaintiff to suffer physical, mental, and economic losses due to the defendants' negligence, totaling 5,000 US dollars. He requests that the defendants be ordered to compensate him. The court accepted the case, and Judge Tu Shenjie summoned the two defendants and their defense lawyer, Wu Pengfei, to court in the Civil Courtroom 7 yesterday morning. First, the plaintiff presented his case. Then, the defendant's lawyer argued that the plaintiff was skilled in boxing. That night, the plaintiff entered the dance hall and was guided by the receptionist Dong Ajin to Seat 86 near the music platform. Before the plaintiff could sit down, he waved the leader of the band to come down from the stage and punched him to the ground when he was unprepared. All the dancers were indignant at this time, and the plaintiff fled. About an hour later, he returned, claiming to be looking for his lost wallet containing 80 yuan. He searched everywhere but could not find it and left. The business of the dance hall suffered considerable losses that night due to his disturbance. The defendant had originally intended to sue him, but because he enjoyed consular jurisdiction, he was still considering whether to proceed. The plaintiff took the initiative and filed a false complaint with the court, requesting compensation. He should be dismissed. The court then summoned witnesses and declared the debate closed, scheduling a ruling in ten days.

The hundreds of chemical abstracts published in each issue are a highlight of the magazine. It is essential reading for chemistry students, teachers, and general researchers. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and cold, with unstable and unsettled conditions and light winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River have relatively strong northerly to northeasterly winds. The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait are cloudy with rain in several places and strong seasonal winds from the north to northeast. The weather around the Ogasawara Islands is very bad due to a hurricane passing through and moving northeast by east. The center of the first hurricane was within 120 miles of 16 degrees north latitude and 137 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM, moving northwest. The wind force is unknown. The center of the second hurricane was within 60 miles of 28 degrees north latitude and 138 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving northeast by east. The wind force is unknown. To the editor: According to Mr. Li Xueqin, manager of Qin Yu Company, the party involved, he claimed that yesterday, upon reading the report "Qin Yu Lane Landlord Cuts Off Water, Tenants Ask for Relief from the City Federation" published on the third page of the Shen Bao on the 3rd of this month, the content was completely inconsistent with the facts and concerned the reputation of the company. The lane rents are low, and as tap water prices rose, the company, bearing the burden, made each room rally to delay rent payment until the water shut off. The matter is concerned with meter installation, is being resolved legally, and is by no means oppressive. The tenant was influenced by someone, thereby turning right and wrong upside down and confusing things. The company requests that the Shen Bao editor uphold justice, investigate the truth, and specially commissions your esteemed lawyer to write to the newspaper for correction. According to this, a corresponding letter is sent, hoping that the newspaper publishes the original letter in the "Letter to the Editor" section for correction. Respectfully, Lawyer Huang Xiubo, July 5th.

Incoming Article: China and the Crisis of the World (3) 202

Dr. Eddy's Speech, Rapidly Recorded by Bingxun Rapid Recording Agency, Shen Wan Rapid Recording

China is now in great danger. Eradicating communism cannot be achieved by simply killing a few heads. We must find the causes and try to eliminate them. These causes are roughly: (1) poverty, (2) unemployment, (3) oppression, and (4) disappointment. I just came from Sichuan. We know that Sichuan is the most abundant and well-irrigated province. There used to be no famine, but now it has become the poorest province. What is the reason for this? (1) The scourge of opium, (2) the warlord system, exploiting the people and even pre-collecting taxes until the 60th year of the Republic, (3) oppression of farmers, and (4) the Communist Party. This time, near the suburbs of Chengdu in Sichuan, I saw many graves, all of whom were communists who had been killed. When I passed through Jiangxi, I met General Kong Hechong. I asked him why he joined the Communist Party and then surrendered to the National Army. He replied, "If a poor child in Hunan has no food to eat at the age of sixteen, then he joins the Communist Party. After receiving six months of education in the Communist Party, the Communist Party calls me to fight. I led the Sixth Army with 75,000 people and captured Changsha. Once I had four million yuan in my hand, but I did not take a penny for myself and distributed it all to the soldiers." I asked him how many people he had killed. He said, "More than 30,000 people." I asked him how he killed them. He said, "First kill the poor to show the rich, to scare them. Line up the captured people, with the poor standing in front, the small and medium rich standing in the middle, and the richest at the end. I would first ask the poor people where the money is. If they answered that they had none, I would cut off their ears and kill them. Later, I also used this method to seize the money of the poor. Even those with ten yuan on them were called capitalists. Salt was sold for one yuan a catty, and cloth was sold for one yuan a foot. Later, I realized that this communist system, in theory and in practice, was not feasible. This principle failed because China does not have large capitalists, only the poor, and everyone can be communist. I felt that this system was the opposite of my original intention to join the Communist Party to save the people, so I left immediately." I believe his words are very sincere. The same method is used in Soviet Russia, but I think it is wrong. We must manage our own homes well before we can manage others. Slaughter is not a good solution. I do not agree with the policy of slaughter. I think the communist danger in Jiangxi was building good roads to suppress the communists. I think suppressing the communists requires educating and guiding them. When I was in Hunan, I found an ancient stele with writings from 3,500 years ago. Although China has such a long history of writing, education is still not widespread. In Japan, nearly 99% of children have received education in the last 30 years, and even coolies can read and write. In Soviet Russia, 90% of children have also enjoyed education within ten years. China had good writing 3,500 years ago, but three-quarters of its people have not received education, and 90% of farmers cannot read and write. They are all struggling in poverty. In North China, the people not only do not have the right to be educated, but some people also take their wheat as taxes. I heard that there are more than 60 kinds of taxes in North China, leaving the people to live in ignorance, lack of knowledge, poverty, and separation. China as a whole is a plate of loose sand, but from an individual point of view, it is very good. The Japanese are not as good as the Chinese. They have very few great people like Ito Hirobumi, but they can unite and cooperate. China cannot cooperate and often has disputes. China has already had 151 civil wars, which is a sign of division and a major cause of national decline. We know that a government cannot always be in revolution. It must unite. I am not saying that the Nanjing government is perfect, or that President Roosevelt's American government is perfect. I am a member of the Socialist Party, and I disagree with him, but I always support him. Now, China's greatest needs can be divided into five categories: (1) education, so that everyone enjoys education, (2) politics, so that we have a clean government, (3) moral strength, (4) economic health, rural construction, and (5) social reform, so that everyone can develop equally. (To be continued)

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

A Contribution

The National Goods Year Cannot Be Blamed on Women 204

— Yang An

This year, the import of cosmetics and perfumes has broken previous records. Everyone is saying that the achievements of the Women's National Goods Year are like this, which is extremely ironic. This view is completely wrong. If this year were not the Women's National Goods Year, would these more than two million dollars worth of cosmetics, perfumes, lace, and jewelry not have been imported? If we didn't promote national goods, could foreign goods not be so rampant? I dare to boldly say that it is fortunate that this year is the Women's National Goods Year, and there is still a group of fools running around, shouting and urging women who do not know how to love their country to use national goods. Otherwise, in this era of rampant human desires and extravagance, I am afraid that the import volume of cosmetics and perfumes would be even greater. In short, people's ridicule is nothing more than indignation, and it does not contain malice. As long as we women strive to make a difference in the future, we will not use any Parisian powder or French rouge. Using national cosmetics and perfumes on the face and body will be worthy of the Women's National Goods Year. If we are willing to admire foreign goods and be ridiculed, then the social sanctions will be very strong. I am afraid that in the future, if someone sees you wearing foreign cosmetics on your face and foreign perfume on your body, they will cover their noses and pass by, scolding you as the most shameless. How can you still show off?

Discussion on National Goods

New Prospects for the National Goods Movement 205

— Shen Si

Next Year Designated as the Student National Goods Year

The National Goods Year has already passed, and the [Women's National Goods Year] is also coming to an end. Although the results of efforts to promote national goods in the past two years have been minimal, especially the increase in imports of goods such as chewing gum, cosmetics, perfume, and toys this year has exceeded our expectations. But can we be discouraged because of this? No, definitely not. Only by intensifying our efforts can we promote and develop the national goods movement. All obstacles and difficulties are inevitable in any [pioneering] work. [The beginning is simple, but the end will be great]. Although the current harvest is not much, success may be in the near future, I believe.

Next year has been designated as the Student National Goods Year. I have endless thoughts about this naming.

Although the dumping of foreign goods is ubiquitous, with their traces everywhere, even in remote areas, the consumption in cities is definitely higher than in rural areas. And goods such as chewing gum, cosmetics, perfume, and toys are even more unrelated to rural areas. The loyal users of national goods are still mostly hardworking farmers. Some of the promoters of foreign goods are educated students. From stationery to clothing, foreign goods often take the place of national goods in schools. This phenomenon is very common and cannot be denied, which is so heartbreaking!

Therefore, in recent years, the central government and the education authorities have repeatedly ordered schools to purchase supplies and student clothing, which must use national goods. Local governments, such as Guangdong Province, have also stipulated that students should use writing brushes and domestic paper as much as possible and are not allowed to abuse pens and foreign paper. However, although the bans are strict, are they not actually [obeyed in appearance but disobeyed in reality] and treated as mere formalities?

Originally, promoting national goods cannot be achieved by any official decree. It is necessary to change the psychology of the general public, cultivate a habit of loving national goods, and gradually promote it, so that it becomes a fashion of the time. This is the only way to achieve practical results. Schools are places to educate citizens, and students are promising young people and the future masters of the country. They should have the courage to [practice what they preach] and take action that is their duty when it comes to promoting national goods and saving the country from danger.

[Past mistakes cannot be admonished], the past mistakes, there is no need to say, and they are unbearable to mention. [The future is still reachable], we can only hope that in the Student National Goods Year of next year, the male and female students in all the large, medium, and small schools across the country will have a sense of self-awareness. In addition to [practicing what they preach], they should also assume the responsibility of doing their best to advocate and urge their families and society. Students are the intellectual class, and they are likely to win the sympathy and belief of the general public. They will definitely be able to bring the national goods movement to a bright path. The significance of [Student National Goods Year] is more profound than [National Goods Year] and [Women's National Goods Year], and the reason lies in this. If it is famous but not real, it would be a disservice to the five words [Student National Goods Year].

At the same time, it is hoped that the school authorities will purchase supplies with strict and accurate amounts, adopting national goods. And national goods factories should also manufacture various educational supplies as much as possible to meet the needs. This is the only way to leave a deep impression on the students. In fact, there are many educational supplies at present that cannot be replaced by national goods, which cannot be considered a major regret. To make up for this regret, we need the efforts of all parties to create a new situation in the coming year and add a special color to the national goods movement.

The Philippine Carnival and National Goods Promotion 206

— Shi Run Shen

Reading the Shen Bao, I learned that Mayor Wu has initiated participation in the Philippine Carnival. I once worked as an editor for the Manila New Fujian Newspaper. I still have some memory of the carnival's impact. And I have a few points to offer regarding overseas national goods promotion. Therefore, I have written this book for the reference of participants.

Every year on February 1, the Philippine government holds a carnival in Manila, P.I. Before the event, Chinese and Western newspapers print election tickets. Cutting them off can be used to elect the carnival queen. The election tickets are sent by various newspapers. The numbers are totaled and published daily in the newspapers. The heat of the election almost reaches 100 degrees on the thermometer, which is beyond the reach of our country's elections.

A few days before the opening, the newspapers will send the queen with the most votes to the association's office for a second election. After the queen is selected, a welcome queen conference will be held the day before the opening. No matter what country you are from, anyone who participates in the conference can register at the association's office in advance. On this morning, costumed welcomers gathered at the venue and marched to the queen's residence to greet her. The queen sat on a three- or four-story-high platform, circumnavigating to the venue. Spectators lined the streets and competed to throw colorful paper strips. When the paper strips were unfolded, they were colorful and beautiful.

The carnival lasts for about two months. During the event, tourists are like weaving and many are in costume. Most people hold paper scraps in their hands and compete to throw them at friends or beautiful women. When the paper scraps are exhausted, they can be bought at the venue. Entrance tickets are sold at the entrance of the venue.

The equipment in the venue displays various items, like an expo.

Overseas Chinese business in the Philippines has always been prosperous. This time, Mayor Wu convened leaders from all walks of life to discuss promoting national goods in the Philippines. I have a few points to offer.

(1) In terms of clothing, domestic serge, spun silk, rayon, and summer domestic women's clothing should be selected, such as the products of Mei Ya, Sanyou, Zhanghua, and other factories.

(2) In terms of food, domestic canned food, candy, biscuits, and preserved plums should be selected, such as the products of Guanshengyuan, Taikang, and Taifeng.

(3) In terms of housing, domestically made beds, tables, chairs, mirrors, bottles, and bedding should be selected.

(4) In terms of transportation, domestically made bicycles, carriages, and cars should be selected. Rickshaws do not need to be transported because the Philippine government prohibits the use of rickshaws. (Ji Ping's note: Before the September 18th Incident, the Liaoning Mortar Factory had self-made many trucks. After the fall of the four provinces, there were no factories in China that continued to make them. (It is regrettable to say this.)

(5) In terms of sports, domestically made sports equipment should be selected, such as the products of the China Standard Company.

(6) In terms of entertainment, domestically made films and musical instruments should be selected, such as the products of the Star and United Film Companies.

The objects to be transported should be as complete as possible. After the closing of the meeting in the future, these objects can be set up as a national goods exhibition hall in the local Chamber of Commerce to be a permanent asset and a memorial. Each item can be sold in the Philippines. This is not a one-time promotion, but a permanent promotion. What do you think of the suggestion to the enthusiastic people involved in trade in Southeast Asia?

National Goods Contribution

The Rise of Domestically Produced Velvet 207

— Huajin

Silk fabrics can originally be divided into three major categories: silk, satin, and velvet. This is how they are classified in all countries, and also how customs classifies silk fabrics. China originally produced all three of these types of silk fabrics. However, only a type of velvet called Zhang velvet was produced. After the 1911 Revolution, imported Western velvet, with its diverse patterns and vibrant colors, became popular. As a result, Zhang velvet gradually declined, and almost no one wore it anymore. Furthermore, very little of it was produced. The reason for its decline was entirely due to a lack of innovation and adherence to outdated methods. Consumers became tired of it over time, and no one cared about it. Moreover, manufacturers failed to improve their technology and equipment, or to imitate Western velvet. Consequently, imported velvet sold well in China, and there was no way to reclaim the economic benefits. The price of imported velvet was as high as ten or more yuan per foot, with a minimum of about one yuan per foot. The extent of this economic drain was unparalleled.

In recent years, domestic silk factories have produced a wide variety of silk and satin products, with many improvements. For example, Meiya Silk Weaving Factory was able to weave high-quality qisha (fine silk gauze) as early as six or seven years ago. However, it was not until this year that silk velvet was produced. This year, several types of domestically produced velvet have become popular in the silk and satin market, such as Yulian Velvet, Meihua Velvet, and Mali Velvet. This is undoubtedly due to the dedicated research of factories like Meiya. In Europe and the United States, velvet is woven two pieces at a time, connected together, and then automatically cut apart by a knife on the machine. However, this type of machinery is extremely expensive, and China does not yet have it, so other methods are used to manufacture velvet. The quality and style of the manufactured velvet is not only similar to that of imported products, but the patterns and colors are also more fashionable and suited to the tastes of the Chinese people.

There is no limit to technology. As long as someone is willing to research and work hard, they will naturally reap the rewards. Domestically produced velvet has now been successfully developed, and many Chinese people are buying it. At the same time, the sales of imported velvet will naturally decrease significantly. This is because the selling price of domestic velvet is only about 30-40% of the selling price of imported velvet, and the quality is the same. Why would Chinese people not want to buy domestic products? Therefore, I believe that to promote domestic goods, manufacturers should first improve the quality and reduce the price, so as to achieve the goal. Forcing people to buy inferior and expensive domestic goods is certainly not a realistic approach.

News About Domestic Goods

Domestic Goods in Nanjing 208

— Wang Shouqiu

㈠ Peddlers and Stall Vendors Prohibited from Selling Foreign Goods

㈡ Barbershops and Cosmetics Must Use Domestic Goods

㈢ National Exhibition Concluded with Excellent Results

Mayor Shi Hengqing of Nanjing is very pragmatic in promoting domestic goods, so the results of promoting domestic goods in Nanjing are very good. The Nanjing Chinese National Goods Company, founded by Mayor Shi, has also been thriving since its opening on Double Ten Day (October 10th), which shows that people in the capital have a considerable understanding of promoting domestic goods. As a result, the atmosphere of using domestic goods is very strong!

Recently, Mayor Shi believed that not only stores should promote domestic goods, but also peddlers and stall vendors. Coincidentally, the Nanjing Social Affairs Bureau is handling the registration of peddlers at the wharf, the Nanjing Public Works Bureau is also handling the registration of stall vendors in the Confucius Temple market, and the Nanjing Health Office is handling the registration of food peddlers. Therefore, Mayor Shi specially instructed the Social Affairs Bureau and the Health Office to require these registered peddlers and stall vendors to sell domestic goods. The relevant bureaus will issue permits only to those who sell domestic goods. If they sell foreign goods, their registration will be immediately cancelled and they will be prohibited from doing business. On the surface, this may seem insignificant. However, if we examine it closely, almost all Eastern goods are sold by these peddlers and stall vendors. Now that Mayor Shi prohibits peddlers and stall vendors from selling foreign goods, the economic losses that can be recovered are indeed considerable. Secondly, the Capital New Life Movement Promotion Association recently noted that the number of imported foreign cosmetics each year is very large. In order to reverse this economic drain, it specially consulted with the Social Affairs Bureau to inform all barbershops in the city that they must use domestic perfumes, cologne, creams, hair tonics, and other cosmetics in the future, and are not allowed to privately purchase foreign goods. In addition, many slogans promoting domestic goods have been made and hung in barbershops to attract the attention of people getting haircuts.

The Capital National Goods Exhibition, organized by more than 160 national goods merchants from Nanjing, Shanghai, and other places, opened on the 20th of last month in the outdoor garden of the Sixiangqiao Great World Amusement Park. It has been going on for a month, so the association closed it down a few days ago. The remaining goods will be partly transported back to the main factory and partly transferred to Wuhu to participate in the exhibition. According to the person in charge of the association, the results of the exhibition were excellent. The revenue from the goods in one month reached more than 200,000 yuan, which is very rare in the current economic downturn!

▲Announcement

The Mad Taoist 209

— Diyin

Chapter One The Mad Taoist Sings the "Good For Nothing Song," Zhen Shiyin Explains the Patriotic Words

It is said that one day, Zhen Shiyin hobbled down the street with a cane, intending to buy some daily necessities for his wife, Feng. Suddenly, he saw a lame Taoist coming from the other side, crazy and unkempt, wearing hemp shoes and a tattered robe, chanting a few lines of verse:

[Chinese people only know that foreign goods are good, they have forgotten about domestic clothing! Dafeng dyeing and weaving has a variety of patterns, Wuhe and Jinglun underwear are good;

Chinese people only know that foreign goods are good, they have forgotten about domestic food! Tiaowei MSG and Weimu, beer and soda are delicious;

Chinese people only know that foreign goods are good, they have forgotten about domestic utensils! Enamel, bakelite, celluloid, and porcelain items are popular;

Chinese people only know that foreign goods are good, they have forgotten about domestic supplies! Yixin toothbrushes and Huasheng fans, Invincible tooth powder is so good;

Chinese people only know that foreign goods are good, they have forgotten about domestic products! Just to mention a few, please remember them, try them and see if they are good?]

Shiyin heard this and stepped forward, saying, "What are you saying, only hearing 'good for nothing, good for nothing'?" The Taoist laughed and said, "If you really heard the words 'good for nothing', then you are considered to understand! You know that our compatriots only think that foreign goods look good, but they don't know that domestic goods are also really good now. My song is called the 'Good For Nothing Song'." As soon as Shiyin heard this, he immediately understood. He laughed and said, "Wait! How about I annotate your 'Good For Nothing Song'?" The Taoist laughed and said, "My song is just a brief overview, please explain." Shiyin then said, "Most Chinese people hold the principle of 'nothing but foreign', thinking that foreign goods must be cheap and good. In fact, this view is extremely absurd! Look at the current domestic factories, their products are excellent and the prices are low. In terms of clothing, the dyeing and weaving products of Dafeng and Dingxin, and the underwear of Wuhe and Jinglun are all well-known. In terms of food, beer, soda, and seasonings are all superior to imported products. Daily necessities include the enamel of the Zhonghua Factory's Lique brand, the bakelite of the Yaguang Factory, and other utensils, the mosquito coils of Samsung and Wudi brands, the electric fans of Huasheng Factory, the light bulbs of Yapuer Factory, the celluloid children's toys of Da Zhonghua Factory, and the straw hats and felt hats of Huafu, the Chinese and American cigarettes. There are truly too many to mention. As for the Sanyou Society, its products are numerous and praised by everyone, so there is no need to elaborate. Good! Think about it: you refuse to use good domestic goods and insist on using things from overseas foreigners, is that not strange? It is truly [recognizing a foreign land as your hometown, how absurd! In the end, you are all making wedding clothes for others!] The mad lame Taoist heard this and clapped his hands, laughing loudly, "Well explained, well explained!" Shiyin then said, "Let's go!" He drifted away with the mad Taoist, causing a commotion in the neighborhood. These words have a point to teach: farmers, workers, merchants, and scholars, everyone is awakened; clothing, food, housing, and transportation, everything is complete. After all, did the mad Taoist lead Shiyin to Shanghai to visit major domestic factories and national goods companies, or did he go to Nanyang to investigate the business of overseas Chinese? There is no explanation in the following text. This chapter is:

The words and phrases are colloquial and amusing, the facts are simple and allow you to guess!

Baseball King Babe Ruth and Others Gave a Brief Demonstration at Shen Garden Yesterday 210

The 22-1 Shanghai Team Was Easily Defeated

The Cold Weather and Small Field Prevented Them from Fully Displaying Their Talents

The Original Ship Departed for the Philippines at 7 PM Last Night 211

The 15 members of the American professional baseball championship team, including baseball king Babe Ruth, arrived here yesterday morning at 9 AM on the Changxing Shipping Company's Empress of Canada. At one point, the welcomers were like madmen. In the afternoon at 2:30 PM, at the invitation of the American Amateur Baseball Association of this port, they held an exhibition match at Shen Garden against the local amateur Mailing and Japanese mixed team. Although tickets were sold for 2 yuan, 3 yuan, and 5 yuan, there were still over a thousand Chinese and foreign people who came to watch, drawn by the reputation. Pictured: Baseball king Babe Ruth and his wife and daughter.

However, due to the strong north wind and sudden cold weather, the players could not display their skills, and the performance was not amazing. The audience also complained endlessly. Although the Shanghai team was composed of elite players, it was no match for the American team. The American team played casually and won 22-1. The one point scored by the Shanghai team was also a gift from the American team. The team left Shanghai on the original ship at 7 PM last night to go to the Philippines.

Record of the Shen Garden Performance 212

The players from both teams arrived at the field around 2 PM. Some Chinese and foreign people specially bought new baseballs and asked the American team players to sign them as souvenirs. They were so busy that they could hardly keep up. Baseball king Babe Ruth was a man of great stature. Although his appearance was fearsome, his conversations and actions were quite humorous. Fox, the new home run king nicknamed Babe Ruth II, was unable to play due to an ankle injury.

Before the start of the game, there were demonstrations of fielding and batting. Any balls hit by the American team that flew over the wire mesh and landed in the stands were snatched by the audience as valuable souvenirs. At one point, more than ten were snatched. This was due to the defense area being too small to be suitable for baseball games. If one exerted too much effort, the ball would definitely go out of bounds. Furthermore, the American team's skills were not fully displayed. Therefore, the game was played casually and there was little excitement. However, the Shanghai team tried their best to attack and defend, but they were still unable to compete.

The American team first performed a demonstration of barehanded fielding. Each person made a gesture of catching and throwing the ball with empty hands. The situation was humorous and earned a lot of applause. The game started at 2:30 PM and lasted nine innings, ending at 4:30 PM. As a result, the American team won 22-1. The Shanghai team allowed the American players to play as they pleased.

The Shanghai team used three pitchers. The first was Mailing's Maris, who had excellent arm strength and deep skill. The American players were at a loss in the first three innings, and were struck out every time. The American team first scored two points in the top of the fourth inning. In the top of the fifth inning, many mistakes were made. High balls and low balls were repeatedly missed, and the situation became chaotic and unmanageable. The Americans scored as many as eleven points. Later, because of his own mistakes, he was taken out of the game. After this inning, Amen Quello was called in as pitcher. He was unremarkable. In the top of the eighth inning, Liepeng was called in. This person was the amateur team's pitcher and the best pitcher in Shanghai. However, because he had not practiced for a long time, his pitches were mostly wild, and the competition became even more dull. The American players were just going through the motions. Biography of Babe Ruth 213

World baseball home run king Babe Ruth was born forty years ago in the city of Baltimore on the American Atlantic coast, near the capital. The city is a desolate little street near the banks of the Baltimore River. Ruth's family was very poor and lived in a dark shack. From a young age, he and his companions played baseball every day. As he grew older, he became particularly interested in baseball. At that time, American baseball games were not as popular as they are now, and there were even fewer youth baseball teams. Moreover, at that time, he was in dire economic straits and had no money to buy a baseball. Therefore, Weiss picked up a tennis ball that others had discarded, and used a wooden hammer as a bat. When there were few horse-drawn carriages on the street, he and some other children played baseball. Because the sports equipment was not complete, the ball could not be thrown far. Each game could not achieve the desired results. However, Ruth was physically strong and stronger than other children, and often hit the ball very far, damaging the glass of nearby fruit shops and grocery stores. The shopkeepers of nearby stores were furious and ordered their clerks to prevent the game every day. Ruth and other children were very afraid of the police. When they saw the police coming, they all ran away. Ruth's parents were very stubborn and wanted Ruth to become a pastor in the future. They worried about Ruth's wandering every day, so they entrusted a young pastor named I. Full group photo of the American baseball team (photo by Zhu Shunlin)

Kilbardi took Ruth to the Skull Religious Academy. One day, Ruth cried bitterly. The reason was not because he was separated from his family, but because the young people on the street could no longer play baseball with him. Kilbardi was very kind and allowed Ruth to exercise freely, so he joined the academy's sports department. Ruth was overjoyed and very happy. Ruth gradually learned to pitch, catch, infield, and outfield. At the age of sixteen, he could throw fast balls with his left hand. Because he was a pitcher, the talented Ruth became even more determined, and his skills improved rapidly. In less than a year, he was hired by the Boston American Supreme Red Inks baseball team as a pitcher. Unfortunately, he injured his left shoulder in that team, so he changed from pitcher to outfielder and specialized in various batting methods. This was the biggest reason for Ruth becoming the world home run king. Ruth has been living on the baseball field for nineteen years from 1915 to the present. His highest annual salary reached 120,000 US dollars. He has played in more than 2,790 games and scored an amazing 708 home runs, making him the world's home run champion. Because of Ruth on this American professional baseball team, audiences flocked to watch their games whether they were in Europe, America, or Japan. His power to attract crowds was greater than that of a generation of emperors.

Home Run Record 214

World baseball king Babe Ruth is from Baltimore, USA, born on February 7, 1894. He is forty years old this year. He first joined the Baltimore Baseball Club as a pitcher, starting his career as a professional baseball player. At that time, Babe was still studying at an industrial school. In 1914, at the age of twenty, he joined the Boston baseball league team in the United States as a pitcher. In 1916, he served as both pitcher and outfielder. In 1920, he joined the New York Yankees for a price of 125,000 US dollars. Ruth's highest salary reached 80,000 US dollars per season. Ruth has been a member of the New York Yankees ever since.

Babe Ruth is the most famous player in American baseball and an idol in the American baseball world. He is one of the most attractive people to spectators. In his lifetime, he has created a total of 708 home runs in the American Baseball League and 15 home runs in the World Baseball Championship. He set a record of more than 50 home runs in four years. In 1927, he even set an unprecedented record of 60 home runs. Ruth is six feet two inches tall and weighs 230 pounds. The number of home runs he has created over the years is listed below:

The China Youth Basketball Association Adds a Women's Championship This Year 217

▲Registration Starts Today

The basketball league hosted by the Shanghai Youth Association has been held for five years. The number of participating teams has increased every year. In order to improve the skills and experience of the teams, the association will continue to hold the league this year and has hired Yue Xiurong (Chairman), Zhou Jiaqi, Liu Xuesong, Wang Yicheng and others as this year's committee members. It is heard that in order to promote women's basketball interest, the association has specially created a women's group. This year, the men's group will also receive two silver balls donated by the Tianjin Chunhe Sporting Goods Manufacturing Factory. The champions of each group will have their names engraved on the balls to commemorate their honor. Those who win the championship for three years will be awarded this cup. The men's group is limited to 60 teams. Registration is encouraged as soon as possible. Please register at the sports department of the association on Sichuan Road. The regulations are attached below:

1) Name: Shanghai China Youth Association Basketball League (referred to as the China Youth Basketball Association).

2) Purpose: To provide all teams with more opportunities to compete, exchange skills, and increase experience and interest.

3) Qualifications: Regardless of school, organization, institution, or company, anyone who is interested in this sport can form a team to participate. However, teams or players who have already joined this year's Western YMCA Basketball Association or the Shanghai Basketball Association are not allowed to join this association. If found, the entire team's competition qualification will be cancelled and the security deposit will be forfeited (the women's group is not subject to this rule).

4) Registration: From now until December 20th. The men's group has a quota of 60 teams. Each team is limited to ten players (the women's group is limited to twelve players). Please submit a photo of the entire team, a registration fee of 2 yuan, and a security deposit of 5 yuan. Players who have not registered and have not submitted photos are not allowed to participate in the competition. Violators will have the competition qualification of the team to which the player belongs cancelled. Furthermore, if a team withdraws or is penalized out of the association, the security deposit will not be refunded, and the competition points obtained will also be cancelled at the same time.

5) Time: The competition time is 5 PM on Tuesdays and Thursdays, and 2 PM on Saturdays. Scheduled dates and times cannot be changed. This does not apply if the date is changed by the association due to force majeure. For each game, teams must arrive within five minutes of the scheduled time. If both parties do not arrive, it will be considered abandonment. Any team that abandons twice will lose its competition qualification and forfeit its security deposit.

6) Court: Each game will be held in the gymnasium of the China Youth Association on Sichuan Road.

7) Groups: The men's group will be divided into business and academic groups, and the women's group will be divided into Group A and Group B. When there are many participating teams, the groups will be further subdivided.

8) Rescheduling: If there are unavoidable accidents that require rescheduling, the association must be notified and permission obtained three days before the game date.

9) Uniforms: Teams without uniforms and players without numbers are not allowed to participate in the competition (unless permitted by the referee).

10) Membership Cards: The men's group will be issued ten player cards per team, and the women's group will be issued twelve. The cards are only valid for entry on the dates when the team has a competition.

11) Prizes: The association will award each group's champion a silver shield. Starting this year, the men's group will be awarded two silver balls donated by the Tianjin Chunhe Sporting Goods Manufacturing Factory. The champions of each group will have their names engraved on the balls to commemorate their honor. Those who win the championship for three years will be awarded this ball.

12) Protests: If a protest occurs, it must be submitted in writing to the committee within 24 hours after the fact, along with a security deposit of 5 yuan. If the committee determines that the protest has sufficient grounds, the security deposit will be refunded; otherwise, it will be forfeited. The committee's decision is final and no further objections will be accepted.

13) Supplementary Rules: The competition rules will adopt the basketball rules promulgated by the Chinese Sports Association from 1934 to 1935.

The French and Chinese Pharmaceutical Football Match Ends in a 1-1 Draw 218

In the Xieling Cup pharmacy football match, France and China-France played yesterday morning at the Public Stadium. The referee was He Chunhui. Death of Mrs. Dawson Scott, Founder of the World PEN Club 222

▲Condolences from the Chinese PEN Club

"PEN Club" is the Chinese translation of (P.E.N. Club). It was initiated in 1921 by an American female writer, Mrs. Dawson Scott, as a writers' dinner party in London. Participants included poets, playwrights, editors, essayists, and novelists. Within a few years, it expanded into an international writers' association, with 34 member countries and 52 branches in various cities. In China, in 1930, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfo, Hu Shi, Zeng Mengpu, Ye Gongchao, Zong Baihua, Xu Zhimo, Xie Shou Kang, Guo Youshou, Zheng Zhenduo, Ge Gongzhen, Lin Yutang, Shao Xunmei, and others initiated the establishment of a branch in Shanghai. One of the PEN Club's missions is that "PEN Club members should make good use of their influence to seek the realization of mutual understanding and respect between nations." The PEN Club's progress over the past decade has been remarkable, and we cannot but thank Mrs. Dawson Scott for her continuous efforts. Therefore, she is called "the Mother of the PEN Club." Unfortunately, Mrs. Scott passed away last month. PEN Clubs in various countries around the world are deeply saddened and have sent telegrams to the London headquarters to express their condolences. It is reported that the Chinese branch of the PEN Club has instructed Guo Zixiong, a member in England, to go and express condolences.

Zhejiang Department of Education Orders the Promulgation of Measures for Liaison Between Middle Schools and Student Families 223

The Zhejiang Department of Education yesterday ordered the promulgation of measures for liaison between secondary schools and student families, ordering compliance. The original measures are recorded as follows: 1. Investigation: 1. Each school should find ways to investigate the student's family situation as a basis for liaison. 2. Communication: 1. At the beginning of the semester, communicate with the student's family about the student's holiday life and homework status. 2. At the end of the semester, communicate with the student's family about the student's academic performance, conduct, sports performance, and the amount of expenses used. 3. After each health check during the semester, communicate with the student's family to discuss ways to correct health deficiencies. 4. If any noteworthy matters concerning the student's health, personality, conduct, academic performance, or other aspects are discovered, communicate with the student's family at any time. 5. Solicit parents' opinions on managing and disciplining their children and improving school facilities. 6. When providing guidance on further education and employment to senior students, solicit the opinions of their parents separately. 3. Visits: If the student's family is not far from the school, regular home visits can be held. If the family is too far from the school and it is necessary, then their guarantor can be visited. 4. Scheduled Talks: If students are found to have noteworthy issues regarding health, personality, conduct, or other aspects, schedule a time to invite their family or guarantor to talk. 5. Invitations to Visit: When the school holds entertainment events, sports meets, health examinations, or achievement exhibitions, student families may be invited to Hangzhou to visit to understand the situation at the school and to use this opportunity to talk with student families to understand the student's family situation and the student's situation at home. 6. Holding Social Gatherings: When necessary, social gatherings are held. Through this, it is possible to understand the student and their family situation, and the family's hopes for the school and the student.

Jinan Aimei Middle School's Grand Martial Arts Drama 226

▲Dispute Between Chairman and Principal Over Performance

A quick message from Jinan states that since Principal Zhou Ai of the private Aimei Middle School resigned, the school's chairman, Hao Fengcheng, has been acting as the principal. However, recently, board members Sun Beitang, Liu Yongshou, Xu Junfu, and others have nominated Pei Yingxi as the principal. Today (2nd), at about 1:00 PM, when Principal Hao Fengcheng was not at the school, Liu Yongshou, Xu Junfu, Xu Jianyuan, Pei Yingxi, and others led more than 20 men and two women to the school to take over. The only person at the school was the director of teaching, Xiang Baokai, who refused to hand over the school. The students also rose up to question them, and a conflict broke out. Two students were beaten and injured, and the doors and window glass of the principal's office were smashed. The new principal, Pei Yingxi, also bled from his right hand, and staff member Li Kuansheng's right arm was also injured. Guo Hai, the chief of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the city, led police to the scene and took them to the branch to mediate before dispersing. It is reported that the Department of Education sent personnel to investigate thoroughly on the 3rd to resolve the issue.

Zhaohe Middle School Commemorates the Zhaohe Uprising and the First Anniversary of the School Yesterday 230

▲Mayor Wu and Director Yang Personally Preside

Zhaohe Middle School, which was established to commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising, held its 15th anniversary of the Zhaohe Uprising and the first anniversary of the school yesterday. The entire day was filled with lively activities. The highlights are recorded as follows:

▲Attendees: School board members Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu; Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan; Municipal Party Representative Yu Zhongbiao; Zeng Zesheng, Wen Yiru, Lu Jie, Wu Depan, etc. from the Security Department, totaling more than 500 people. They were warmly received by the school principal Jia Botao and Zhu Jiarang, Yao Sufang, etc.

▲Inspection: At 9:00 AM, Mayor Wu and Director Yang arrived together on time, welcomed by the music of the police garrison headquarters. Then Director Pan Gongzhan also arrived. There were many guests, so the inspection began. The vanguard was the military band of the police garrison headquarters, followed by the student army and then the Boy Scouts, all neatly dressed and with a strong military appearance. Lianhua Yihua Company filmed the event.

▲Meeting: Then the Boy Scouts performed a fire drill with fire extinguishers from Pushi Industrial Company and inspected internal affairs, including classrooms and bedrooms. Wu, Yang, Pan, and others personally inspected them. Because the school implemented militarization, it was neat and simple, resembling a model barracks. At 10:30 AM, the meeting officially began. Chairman Yang Hu respectfully read the will and presented flowers. Then he reported on the Zhaohe Uprising. Then Mayor Wu delivered a speech in his capacity as chairman, and Director Pan Gongzhan of the Education Bureau gave a speech. Finally, Principal Jia gave a speech of thanks.

▲Speeches by Wu and Pan: The mayor's speech briefly stated that the Zhaohe Uprising was the most glorious page in the history of the revolution, which can promote the completion of the revolution and the unity of the party. Therefore, we should use various methods to commemorate and promote it. The establishment of this school is to use the spirit of the martyrs to cultivate students, so that the students of this school not only gain knowledge but also can contribute the spirit of the martyrs to society. Director Pan briefly stated that the Zhaohe Uprising was the harbinger of the National Revolution. However, the work of the Kuomintang now is to overthrow imperialism, which requires the power of the entire nation and youth. The revolutionary atmosphere of Zhaohe Middle School is stronger than other schools. It is hoped that students will strengthen their physical strength, intelligence, and morality in preparation.

▲Grand Entertainment Performance: At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, there was a sports meet, at 6:30 PM a parents' meeting, and at 8:00 PM an entertainment performance. More and more guests and student parents arrived. The program included piano solos, solo singing, string duets, and four-part choruses, which were performed by colleagues from the National Conservatory of Music and Yale, as well as many wonderful dramas and Ping operas.

▲Publication of a Special Issue: The school originally planned to publish a Zhaohe Overview, but because the content was too complicated and the printing was not enough, it had to be published a few days later. A commemorative special issue was published by the Social Evening News and was distributed with the newspaper yesterday.

Municipal Education Bureau Forbids the Filming of Supernatural and Strange Films 233

▲Request the Central Government to Pay Close Attention

▲Send Bureau Staff to Conduct Thorough Searches

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has always paid close attention to assisting the Central Government in inspecting films. Recently, the bureau has received reports from various sources that many film companies in the city are secretly filming supernatural and strange films, such as "Lu Chunyang Plays Three Times with Bai Mudan" and "Riot in the Crystal Palace," which are all promoting superstition and have a significant impact on the nation and society. In addition to reporting to the Central Government for close attention, the bureau also yesterday

instructed all film companies to comply. The original order is as follows: It has been found that the production of supernatural and strange films has long been prohibited. However, in order to seek profit, some film merchants have not hesitated to circumvent the laws and still secretly film them from time to time, which is a violation of the ban. The bureau has reported this several times and forwarded it to the Central Film Inspection Committee for attention. The Film Inspection Law promulgated by the Legislative Yuan strictly restricts films from taking superstition and supernatural subjects as themes. Shanghai is the center of the country's film industry, and the bureau's duty lies in urging its subordinates to conduct thorough searches and confiscate and destroy any supernatural and strange films to uphold the law and prevent their spread. All film production companies should also understand the government's painstaking efforts to protect the domestic film industry. If any film studio is borrowed to film such films, they should refuse or secretly report it to the bureau without any hesitation.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise 240

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Flattering Smiles Meet the Lamp's Glow, Haggard Hunger Drives on, Powdered Faces Learn to Be Charming

Auntie Hu initially blushed, then turned into a smile, saying, "I'm not blaming you. I'm just saying, with the young lady right here, it's embarrassing for you to say such things." As she spoke, she reached out and pulled Yueying inside, laughing, "Come in, don't just stand there half in and half out. You're just attracting attention." After being pulled inside by her, Yueying immediately sat down on a square stool in the corner by the wall. There was a small two-drawer table here, with paper, cigarettes, matches, teacups, torn paper, pen and ink, and other things scattered on top. There were also two things that the poor couldn't bear to look at: a large cornbread and a plate of stir-fried leeks with shredded meat. Moreover, there was a pair of chopsticks on the plate, as if it were prepared for someone to eat. Auntie Hu smelled the aroma and had already swallowed her saliva. She pinched off a small piece of cornbread, as if joking, and put it in her mouth to chew. Little Ji ignored her and asked, "What kind of powder is she wearing on her face?" He nodded his chin towards Yueying's face. Auntie Hu said, "We don't have rouge and powder in our house. This is a little bit of leftover tooth powder that I let her put on." Little Ji said, "Auntie Hu, this is freshly baked cornbread, is it delicious?" Auntie Hu pinched off another small piece and laughed, "It's good! Are you offering it to me?" Little Ji said, "What's this? I'll treat both of you. But there's one condition, you have to agree to do one thing for me. We have female guests here. I'll go borrow some rouge and powder and you and this young lady can doll yourselves up a bit. Maybe I can even borrow a dress..." Yueying lowered her head and rushed to say, "I won't!" Little Ji didn't look at her, but looked at Auntie Hu. Auntie Hu said, "Just this little piece of cornbread, you're treating it like it's so important." Little Ji said, "Don't rush, since I'm treating you two, of course I'll let you two eat your fill. I have more." As he spoke, he took out a cornbread from a small basket under his bed and a can of pickled mustard tuber that was already opened, with half of it still inside. He laughed, "There's hot tea in the pot on the table, pour it yourself. I'm going to borrow some things." As he said this, he darted away in a flash. (82)

Street Artists 241

— Zhu Ying

Street artists are not from art schools, let alone studying at some academy in Paris. They don't know what is called art for art's sake, let alone what is called culture. But they have a good ability to create images.

Snippets 242

— (A' Yuan)

There is a saying in the Suzhou and Shanghai area: "Blowing cowhide." Pi (皮, "hide") is a euphemistic representation of a vulgar word, although slightly more elegant, it is not really understandable. I think that in the future, when writing articles and wanting to quote this phrase, it can be rewritten as "Comparing a mouse to an ox," which is more humorous and unconventional. This is because the pronunciation of "blowing" (吹) and "mouse" (鼠) are similar in the Suzhou and Shanghai dialect; and using the smallness of a mouse to compare with the largeness of an ox still retains the original meaning of self-aggrandizement.

Street artists create images, not using plaster, nor do they use knives for carving. All that street artists have is a ball of colorful cooked flour. Their tools are a bamboo sliver, a broken small wooden comb with no more than ten teeth, and a ball of old cotton soaked in vegetable oil.

The ten clumsy and rough fingers of the street artist can create delicate human figures. They can all use oily fingers and the strength of a bamboo sliver to knead and sculpt the colorful cooked flour into different images. Guanyin Bodhisattva, Ji Gong the Monk, Indian Asan, foreign women, as well as clam spirits and silk factory girls, can all be sculpted vividly and lifelike.

Street artists are wanderers on the streets, but they also rely on their skills to live. Ji Gong the Monk sells for ten coppers, the clam spirit sells for sixteen coppers. Although their works are not taken to Zhibo or salons for promotion and exhibition, the street artists are perfectly aligned with the saying "art for life."

Of course, Ji Gong the Monk, Guanyin Bodhisattva, and the like are too naive and humble, not as popular as the statues of historical figures created by great artists, but I think this is a faithful representation of the culture of the common people in our country.

Moving from Old Houses to New Villages 243

— Lu Danlin

In recent years, general real estate developers in Shanghai have felt that the names of the houses they used to build, such as "fang" (坊) and "li" (里), are somewhat rigid and fail to attract people's attention. Therefore, many newly built houses have been renamed "villages" (村) or "villas" (别墅), hoping to change people's perceptions. In reality, it is still the same wine in a new bottle.

The houses in the alleyways of the li and fang are all the same, which is really annoying. The air is bad, the light is bad, and the construction of the houses is simple and rigid. Although some have become slightly more modern recently, the rent is at least one or two hundred yuan per month, or at least seven or eight thousand yuan. If you are not afraid of the high rent and are willing to live in an environment with polluted air, its organization and spirit are extremely scattered. It can be said that there is no organization at all, except when opposing rent increases by the landlord.

New villages are different. They are a sound and concrete group. The house style and roads, flower gardens, guards, water and electricity, fire protection, cleaning, and elementary schools, assembly halls, etc., are all carefully designed by experts, and the facilities are adapted to local conditions to ensure that the families living in the village have a very comfortable life. This kind of life is definitely not something that can be dreamed of in the messy alleyway houses in the city.

Now, fortunately, the Rose Garden New Village has appeared in Shanghai. We often curse the tenants living in the old-fashioned alleyway houses in the li and fang. If you are determined to try the real new village life, it is better to join the Rose Garden New Village and work together. They are adopting the nature of a cooperative to manage the new village's business. Everything in the village is done according to the principles and spirit of cooperation. Mutual assistance in vigilance, mutual support in illness, mutual respect and mutual assistance are indeed a special force in the New Life Movement. They are definitely not like the old-fashioned alleyway houses where people treat each other like people from Yue treating people from Qin, indifferent to each other's prosperity or decline, and each minding their own business.
