Naval Discussion 245

— Yin Juan

Rainbow Clouds Song 246

— Sun Choucheng

Sai Jinhua, living in poverty in Beiping, has recently had a biography written about her by famous figures, and funds have been raised to maintain her life, attracting attention. According to reports, when Sai Jinhua first entered the brothel, she hung a plaque that read "Fu Caiyun." After being housed in a golden house by Hong Zhuangyuan (Hong Jun), she went to Germany with him. After Hong died, she returned to the brothel and changed her name to Sai Jinhua. During the Gengzi Incident (Boxer Rebellion), because of her old friendship with the German commander Waldersee, she persuaded him to restrain his subordinates, protecting many lives and properties, and people were grateful for her virtue, respectfully calling her "Second Master Sai." Her power and influence were once so great, but now she is so destitute, one cannot help but feel the lament of a beauty in her twilight years. Fan Fanshan Fangbo and Wang Biyun Xiaolian both wrote Rainbow Clouds Songs at that time. Fan's work was printed and widely recited, while Wang's work was not easily shown to others, and few knew about it. Choucheng is from the same hometown as Wang and has kinship ties. He was shown it in the past, and I cherish the remaining manuscripts. I am publishing them here specifically for reference.

(Rainbow Clouds Song has an introduction) During my time in Tianjin, I heard the name of Sai Jinhua. During my holidays, I went to see her with my friends. I arrived while she was still doing her morning makeup, and she came out after a long delay. As soon as she came out, the whole room came alive. The six guests in the room all received her perfect attention. Though old, she was still as beautiful as a young girl, truly a rare beauty. In the past, a certain minister, who was sent to Germany, had a concubine named Caiyun, who was known for her beauty. The German Empress loved her and took a small photo with her. The Empress was the son of Queen Victoria of England, who was also beautiful. The high favor shook Europe, and the matter spread overseas. Caiyun was originally a singer in Suzhou. After the minister died, she was restless and returned to the brothel, and changed her name to Sai Jinhua. I could not help but feel moved, and I imitated the Changqing style to write this poem, not only to record the rare beauty and weave in current affairs, but also to warn future generations.

Leaving the brothel and moving the orchid boat, the boat girl's slender hands skillfully stir the soup, the flower fragrance is so pleasant, the mountain scenery across the bank is so beautiful, there is an appointment with the neighboring girl to play, the young master sends a poem while traveling, the morning comb is decorated with a jade hairpin, the clever maid cheers and knows the trick. The child was born on the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival, and Caiyun holds up the moonlit galaxy. The small characters are picked up, the mother pities, only allowing a fairy to ride in the future. Born beautiful and living in Hengtang, sitting in front of the flowers every day, competing for beauty, still charming in her youth, her name fragrant everywhere in the spring breeze, hearing her name but wanting to know her face, who knew that seeing her would break the heart, a guest in the Golden Palace before ten thousand miles, a jade flute girl on the Three Lives Stone. The embroidered carriage should be welcomed early, but Longgang still needs to be expressed, the wife is easy to find because of love, the ministers dare not lightly abandon the etiquette, suffering the secret friends to hide the beauty, the golden house secretly builds the magpie bridge, it is expected that the zither will not be in tune, measuring her embrace, a pitiful night. In the blink of an eye, another year, leaving the hometown trees, flying together to Yantai, the husband waits for the dawn, the maid smokes incense in the painted pavilion, the king chooses an envoy to be gentle, the phoenix decree is sent, the emperor sings the song, singing far away for thirty thousand miles, and the boudoir turns into the worry of the concubine, but teaching the little wife to follow, good at learning from the lady, do not be careless. A new purple haze pendant is given as a special gift, and the crows fly into the blue phoenix team, the traveling knight with a curly beard recognizes Li Lang and Hong Fu Mei. Translating the barbarian's tongue, she is skilled in the art of Kucha in a foreign country, the flower branches are only displayed in Berlin, and the pear orchard sings the ballad of Luo Fu. The fairy of the Jade Palace loves her gracefulness, the doctor welcomes her with incense, cunningly concealing the majesty of the phoenix, the crystal clear glass illuminates the shadow of the swan, from then on, her demeanor spreads overseas, and a new chapter opens with the fortunate journey of the star carriage, the star carriage returns to the imperial capital, buying a map for a thousand gold, the cunning merchant deceives, turning an inch of mountain and river into a thousand miles. The old friend is the same in the past, but the hand turns repeatedly without end, and Shu Road changes everywhere, the human being is divided into the heart and the ghosts, but he is worried about sleeping in the rain, and the empty bed of the wanton woman is difficult to guard alone, singing loudly of the red phoenix coming in the clouds, whispering about the Qin Palace in the flower bed. Nothing is left but a long sorrow, thirst quenches the garden, Yan Zi does not live in Guan Panpan, the old dream warms in the light of the lantern, the new knowledge is made by the scholar, the light song and slow dance are still happy, changing the feathers and moving the palace. All things rise and fall, the wheels turn, a dream is absurd, the bananas are overturned, and suddenly the sacred fire amazes the god of the barbarian clothes, and the yellow turban in the river in competition to the shores bow to Zhang Jiao, the drums of the confederation shake the earth, the orioles and flowers in the rapids follow the wind, a general flies from outside the sky, and the gold hairpin is reunited, the fine horse on the seven-treasure carved saddle, the nine-hua brocade is inhabited by a pair of mandarin ducks. The two palaces are hunted in the west, the sound of the market is broken, the upper kingdom's clothes are covered in charcoal, the jade ring prince weeps on the roadside, and the golden fish is taken by the courtier. The locked-bone Bodhisattva is heartbroken, and begs for mercy from the general every time, the prime minister gives peace and倾 pours out the treasury, and the barbarians are full of desire to prepare their whips, the galloping wheels are about to leave, whispering farewell, the pearl tears fall lightly, the smoke of the beacon is scattered, the chariot returns to the capital, and the prosperous atmosphere is still as before, the young heroes of Wuling indulge in extravagance, and a song of entanglement is innumerable. The beauty is changing people, and the old lady is still charming, filling the room with beautiful men for self-entertainment, allowing you to break your heart and ask about your failures, the white and tender skin is just grotesque, and the red face is abruptly cut off by the fish girl's blade, the wind and rain of jealousy darkens Chang'an, the iron-cast document is written in snow, and the back of the document shows from the clerk, the jujube village still relies on the joy of the song, the criminal court is easy to turn around, the evil sea is difficult to stir the rudder, the purple street is thick with spring songs, the flowers bloom and fall from Jiangnan. (This song was written in the year of Xin You, so the matters of remarrying Weissan and changing her name to Wei Zhao Lingfei, etc., are not included.)

Records of Fragrant Mists 247

— Original work by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

Indeed, the portrait does not tell us in such detail: it tells us of a large glass case, which is placed right below the portrait, and inside are all the clothes of the person in the painting: his Mongolian saddle, his exquisite hunting suit, his pure gold stirrups, all complete. What's missing is the living person and the living horse. According to my speculation, the author of that portrait must have based it on these real things, first drawing a shell, and then recalling the appearance and identity of the owner of these things, carefully adding them, and then piecing together this moving portrait.

There are also three things on the painting that have not been mentioned above. The first is a leather whip hanging on Qianlong's left hand; the second is a bow on his left hand; and the third is a quiver with several arrows inserted in it. These three things are also displayed in the same large glass case, so we can also appreciate them carefully. The leather whip is about three feet long, one end is braided with several leather straps like braids, which is used to drive the horses; the other end is a white jade handle, with two small holes drilled through it, and another silk ribbon is tied to it, so that the hand can be put into the silk ribbon, so that it can be swung at will. Looking at the arrows and bows, they are generally inlaid with white jade. I can't help but wonder if the arrowheads made of white jade can really be used for hunting? Perhaps these arrows are just decorations, and iron arrowheads are used instead when they are actually used. (192)

Grains: 期粉 (Future Flour) Has 空抵補 (Short Covering) 261

Yesterday in the flour market, after opening in the morning, the market for each month showed an initial flat and then stable appearance. 洋麥 (Foreign Wheat) quotations: Chicago rebounded by about 24 jiao, and Canada rose by 8 fen to about 2 jiao. When pricing, the industry was not active, and market sentiment inside and outside the industry was not active. Therefore, the opening market appeared weak. Then, with 空抵補 (short covering), the factory slightly sold the distant months, with little other activity. As a result, the opening price gradually improved again. Until the afternoon opening, this month, due to the end of the lunar year accounting, customer transactions were quite settled. Temporary 空抵補 (short covering) was very strong, so the market improved again. According to the current situation, it will become a mutual deadlock, and there will be little huge ups and downs. As a result, this month to February each improved by 1.75, March and April rose by 2.5 fen, and May rose by 2.25 fen.

As a result, the volume of transactions in the market has been decreasing day by day. Free Talk

On Realistic Literature 285

— Can Yue

Recently, I read Mr. Qi's article "Realistic and Romantic" published in this section. It elaborates the relationship between realism and creative imagination or fantasy in a quite detailed manner, which is very helpful for people to deeply contact and understand the vastness of the realistic literary structure. Although realism has been talked about a lot, it is generally believed that realism still remains on objectivism. This purely objectivist interpretation drags the free and broad realism into a shallow quagmire. Here, I would like to describe several characteristics of realistic texts, or perhaps it can make the relationship, similarities and differences between realism, romanticism and factualism clearer.

Romantic writers purely subjectively describe personal private life, or develop personal whims and fantasies; factualist writers purely objectively describe reality from a bystander's perspective; unrealistic fantasies of romanticism naturally depart from their own social practice, and the purely objective descriptions of factualism also separate social practice from themselves. Therefore, both romanticism and factualism have biases. However, realistic literature is not like this. It does not simply value either one or the other, but integrates and activates real life and personal ideals. Realistic observation cannot be effective with pure objectivity. Personal fantasy or romantic elements should also permeate from reality. Therefore, the "human" nature described by realism is a social type, a lively personality with objective conditions. The social phenomena described are dynamic parts, not static and dead things.

Realism does not reject idealistic elements; it needs lively ideals to illuminate the historical trend of reality. Therefore, the description of psychology is even more urgently needed. However, the psychological description of the characters' personalities should be described as a typical psychology in the development of the environment, rather than starting from the individual's psychological perspective to narrate the social development in the story (whether real or imaginary). In other words, the author should understand the generality and particularity of individual psychology from the unfolding of facts and the changes in the real environment, and analyze the individual psychology from the dynamic state of reality. If one does not base on the progress of reality and only relies on personal fantasy, that is the ethereal and empty fantasy of romanticism. This subjective view makes the content of the work stained with empty emphasis. As a result, many formulaic works that distort reality have made mistakes in this regard.

Realism should use a correct worldview to dissect realistic themes. The author unfolds the dynamic posture of reality from the story and carefully grasps the correct part. First; the author must see the development process of society, and the various fundamental forces that promote this process and determine this development. Not only should they explain it, but they should also consciously recognize that advancing trend. Therefore, realistic works are definitely no longer things that expose something. Second; the realistic view cannot be superficial, but should deeply understand the unity of internal opposites. One cannot regard the unity of opposites as the sum of examples. The process of social development contains phenomena that contradict and reject each other. Intercepting a period of the process in its own movement still contains a chaotic division, as well as further unity and opposition. This must be grasped from the dynamic aspect of society.

Mouse (Part 2) 286

— Lu Fen

Being bitten in one's shoes is considered unlucky by superstitious people, especially officials who are most taboo about it. After everyone washed their faces in the morning, there was still time before mealtime, so they would light a cigarette and chat as usual. But at mealtime, the "chimney" was nowhere to be seen, and everyone thought he had gone to buy shoes. So they talked about shoes, and the meal tasted particularly delicious than usual. When everyone returned to the room, they saw the "chimney" sitting alone, staring intently under his bed.

"What's wrong, are you so angry that you didn't even eat, Chimney?"

Another person lit a "post-meal cannon," glanced contemptuously at "Chimney," and chimed in: "Hmph, buying a pair of shoes," made a face, and lay down on the bed, yawning from oversleeping.

"Chimney's" nickname originally came from bragging, but at this time, he unexpectedly remained silent. The others were very excited, and all these officials recognized that a terrible daytime had already begun. The room was filled with smoke, some pacing, some sitting at their desks drawing circles, and adding two ink circles as eyes next to a person's name, and finally, someone laughed to themselves and finished. Everyone was silent for a while. Because of widespread indigestion, there was often a loud sucking sound amidst the smoke. Suddenly, a "squeak, squeak" sound called out from somewhere. "Chimney" dived into his bed like a tiger, and seemed to shout something like:

"Tickling the tiger's head, wearing a long gown will eventually attract customers! Run, run? You can't run away!"

At the same time, a cage woven from thorns and bamboo rolled out with him. A mouse squeaked and rushed around inside, not caring about hurting its head because it wanted to break free. "Chimney" held the mouse cage high above his head, jumping around outside, and seemed to shout something, but it was not clear in the commotion, probably something very heroic.

But a question came up: how to deal with this captured prisoner?

I remember that when I was a child, whenever I caught a mouse, I would rush to find a cat in every neighbor's house. Cats are insidious and cunning things, very fearful of getting into trouble. Even if you visit his grass hut thrice, he may not willingly be captured, so in order to find a cat, people often spent half a day racking their brains. It was probably because "the more labor, the greater the joy," and when they finally managed to invite a cat teacher, they were not only happy enough to shed tears, but they simply wanted to dance with joy. That was a very interesting game, called "cat's tail hanging." The mouse was tied to the cat's tail with a rope, so that the cat could not bite the mouse. Then the cat was released, and the show began: the cat hooked its head back and wanted to eat the mouse, the mouse was so scared that it cried "goo goo," the cat was even more afraid that the mouse would bite its tail, and wanted to eat it quickly, so it spun around, and the "meow meow goo goo" sounds mixed together, until everyone was tired of it. Although this cruel prank was not very "humane," the children did not care much.

Officials were no longer children. When the time came to exercise their power, they would always come up with new tricks. After a small dispute, everyone finally agreed: to light a sky lantern. In fact, this trick was not new, but it was just an old punishment previously applied to people, and now it was used on mice.

At a certain period, humans were cruel and loved killing. When there was no one to sacrifice, they turned to animals. This was a very spectacular execution. Everyone waited, and dusk finally arrived. Everyone gathered in the open space behind the yamen, waiting to cheer for the last time. Although it was just a mouse, the situation was almost the same as watching a murder.

A mouse covered in kerosene, lit with fire, was not without its grandeur. It could be seen rolling and running in the open space like a ball of fire, making a shrill squeaking sound. It ran and rolled, and just as it was moving forward vigorously, it suddenly turned back, seemingly wanting to find a comfortable cave to hide in. Even a negligible life still knew how to escape, even though it clearly knew that it was on fire and everything was hopeless. After ten minutes or perhaps only a few minutes, amidst the cheers of people stamping their feet, it could not help but stop struggling and fall down. It reached a burial place where even finding water wouldn't give a peaceful burial.

After this, the mouse's momentum was greatly reduced. Although it still galloped on the ceiling, because the number of family members was sharply reduced, it was not as rampant as before. There were even fewer who dared to come out for a leisurely stroll. The "lighting sky lanterns" execution could still be seen every night, but it no longer had the initial excitement, and some people preferred to sit by the window and watch the lanterns.

Naturally, the rats were still not completely eradicated. The person called "Chimney" was dismissed for dereliction of duty, and on the eve of his departure, he seemed to say resentfully:

"Rats, rats! There are many heroes in the world who fall (note) into the mouths of rats!"

Such a hero could not forget his bitten shoes. Soon the mousetrap also disappeared, and the rats became rampant again, and gradually dared to walk on the tables and under the tables.

(Note) "Fall" means to fall down. An abbreviation of "fall."

[Zikai's Cartoons, My Collection] Preface 287

— Lu Sun

Because I enjoyed reading the articles in the "Free Talk" section of the Shenbao newspaper, I kept each issue as it came out. Recently, I sorted them and bound them into three large volumes, and even drew what I thought were very beautiful designs for their covers. Furthermore, I used a knife to carefully cut out each of Mr. Zikai's cartoons that were published inside. Then, I bought some gray cardstock, folded it into pages the size of a sixteenmo book, and pasted two cartoons onto each page. In this way, I created a separate album. I also drew a cover for it and titled it "Zikai's Cartoons, My Collection."

Speaking of which, I seem to be a person with a ["collecting癖"] (?), but what I collect is limited to the books and newspapers that I enjoy. Therefore, I preserve every newspaper supplement that I like, keeping it completely intact and binding it in a way that I find very aesthetically pleasing. I remember that this habit began way back in my first year of middle school, inspired by the "Awakening" section of the Shanghai Min Guo Daily; since then, this practice has never stopped. However, those early works were lost at a friend's place in Shanghai and were destroyed in the ["January 28th Incident"] fire, which I still deeply regret!

Regarding this troublesome collecting work, many friends have asked me in the past: What is the meaning of all this? I couldn't answer, so I could only vaguely say, "I like it."

In reality, I am not a scholar, not a specialized researcher. I do this work with no particular ambition or agenda. Besides occasionally flipping through it myself, it's simply because I like it, I'm interested, I enjoy doing it; I just want to do it.

But since Mr. Zikai's cartoons are published in the "Free Talk" section, why did I have to cut them out one by one and bind them into a separate album? There are several other reasons.

First, because of my special love for Zikai's cartoons.

Second, in my collection of "Free Talk" issues, there are a total of over sixty of Zikai's cartoons, from early exploratory works to the "Wonton Noodle Vendor," which I thought was enough to bind into an album.

Third, it's more enjoyable to look at this way.

If you were to ask me why I have such a special fondness for Zikai's cartoons, it's not only because Mr. Zikai's painting skills are so profound; what I love most is the subject matter of the paintings and the content within.

This reminds me of a deep impression that has not faded to this day, which is my initial understanding of Zikai's cartoons. This impression came from a cartoon Mr. Zikai made for ["Middle School Student"] magazine more than four years ago. At that time, I was still a middle school student; even now, without closing my eyes, I only need to think for a moment, and the cartoon appears clearly before me: a young man wearing glasses and Western-style clothing, carrying books and stationery, striding briskly past a sorrowful young man, burdened with a heavy wonton noodle carrying pole; besides the signature "TK," there was a title that read "Classmates from Elementary School Days."

That cartoon plunged me into a very long, deep contemplation, almost indistinguishably merging with the image: it made me think of the elementary school classmates I encountered when I returned home for the holidays; some had become peddlers, some had become laborers, some... In this way, it gently sowed seeds of sadness in my heart; however, I felt that this sadness was a beneficial ["comfort"] to my spirit.

["Because Feng Zikai's paintings are indeed simple and easy to understand on the surface, lacking any mystery or novelty, the meaning within the paintings is not superficial. Where does it not reveal life? Take a moment to savor it, and you will discover your own sorrows and vexations, and feel that the painting can be a spokesperson for your sorrows."]

丨Excerpt from Zhou Qi's ["On Feng Zikai"].

The characters and events that appear in Zikai's cartoons are all familiar; the lines in the paintings are always so simple, everyone can understand them, and everyone who sees them feels a burst of inexplicable relaxation in their heart, and it easily leaves you with a clear and bright impression.丨This is Mr. Zikai's greatest success.

In addition to making cartoons, Mr. Zikai is also a master of writing short essays; reading his short essays is as pleasant and flavorful as reading his cartoons. Therefore, his ability to write short essays also helps his cartoons,丨often making the titles of the paintings so good; sometimes it precisely compensates for the inadequacy of his simple compositions.

Take the sixty-odd cartoons that I have collected, for example, almost every one of them relies on his appropriate titles to further enhance the perfection of the painting's meaning.

Like "A Boy and A Dog," "99th Beat," "Their Sofa," "Sanitary Equipment," "Variety and Unity," etc., all have profound humor.

"Eastern Neighbors Offer Condolences, Western Neighbors Offer Congratulations," "The May Thirtieth Song," "The Ratio of Three to One," etc., all express profound satire.

"You Peel a Melon for Me, I Fan You," "Take It Down," "We Are Going to Welcome the Lantern Festival," etc., further express the innocent childlike heart of children. "Green and White," "Willow Shade," etc., are simply a beautiful essay, a poem with harmonious rhythms.

And "Destination," "Selling Broth," "Barber's Pole," "Cooling Off," "Sugar Cake," "Rickshaw," "Do You Want to See," etc., are all quick sketches taken from our environment and things around us. When we look at these quick sketches, we cannot help but be aroused to great interest and attention in the circumstances of life.

There are also those scenes of rural life, as well as those old-fashioned life situations that still exist in the countryside, which have almost been forgotten by us who have lived in the city for a long time, or even never known about. Mr. Zikai, however, uses his artistic brush to leave them a permanent memorial. Such as: "The Two-Stringed Instrument," "Fifth Sister-in-Law," "The Herdboy and the Weaver Girl Stars," "Southern Fields," "Talking About Hemp," etc.

In addition, there are realistic portrayals of tragic events, such as: "Distributing Gruel," "Offering Tea," "Clouds and Rainbows," "Eighty-Seven Years Old," etc., all of which are deeply touching works.

After pasting Mr. Zikai's cartoons, I also cut out a photo of Mr. Zikai from the "Second Anniversary Issue of The Analects" and pasted it at the beginning of the album; I pasted Zhou Qi's "On Feng Zikai," from the "Free Talk" section, at the end.

In this way, this collection of mine is considered complete.

Although it won't be published, this album will surely be borrowed and looked at by friends; they will inevitably ask me again, What is the meaning of doing this kind of work? To avoid the trouble of repeatedly answering in words, I feel it necessary to write a preface.

Therefore, I have written the above words as a self-preface.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Studying Dead Books and Reading Dead Books (Part 2) 290

— Chui

What does it mean to read dead books? Reading dead books and studying dead books are not the same. Perhaps the materials being read are not good, or perhaps the method of reading is not correct, then even a living book becomes a dead book. Therefore, reading dead books can be explained in several ways.

1. It means swallowing information whole without digesting it, being unable to apply it.

2. It means reading completely useless books, or even harmful books.

3. It means flipping through books randomly, looking at whatever, without any system.

The first type was common among scholars in our country in the past; that is why there were xiucai (successful candidates in the imperial examination) who could not even write a simple note. The second type also has many drawbacks, such as the recent phenomenon of students being fond of reading martial arts novels, or supernatural novels, or romance novels, leading to bizarre events such as four apprentices from a rice shop in Wuxi suddenly disappearing, claiming to have gone out to seek enlightenment. As for the third type of problem, it is even more common; I myself suffer greatly from this problem, so my reading makes no progress and brings no benefit.

Reading must have a purpose, be orderly, and be systematic. Because books are as numerous as sweat could dampen, not only the ancient books of our country are too many to read, but now, with the addition of foreign books, there is even less energy and time to examine them one by one. One can only take the books that one wants to study and likes to study, and study them. In the past, our country's scholars included ["experts in Confucian classics,"] historians, ["experts in Neo-Confucianism,"] essayists, ["textual critics,"] ["commentators,"] and ["etymologists,"] etc., most of whom focused on one type of learning and studied it diligently. They were right about their method of studying learning, but unfortunately, the objects of their study cannot be said to be completely useless, but many did waste their energy and work hard for no gain. This method of study is the same method used by foreign scholars to study ["philosophy,"] ["science,"] ["psychology,"] ["law,"] ["sociology,"] etc., but the objects of study are divided into ["dead"] and ["alive"].

This statement is entirely for those who read for the sake of reading, for those who read to study learning. But how many people in our country have this energy and this leisure? In addition, there are those who read to become officials, those who read to do business, those who read to find a job in society, and those who read to simply be on a school roster, and these are in the majority. They can only take commonly used books and study them, which is another kind of reading method.

Reading in the private school style is naturally different from reading in the school style. Reading in the private school style is too bitter, while reading in the school style is too sweet. The private school style spends too little time on reading, which is certainly not suitable. But the school style wastes too much time on reading, which is also a pity. Currently, going to school costs so much that it is not easy for families to bear, not to mention the long ["winter vacation,"] ["spring vacation,"] and ["summer vacation"]. In a week, there is a ["Sunday"] holiday, as well as ["various commemorative"] days and ["sports meets,"] etc. The time spent reading in a year is only half of what it could be, which is such a pity!

Some say that private schools teach dead books, while schools teach living books, but I am afraid that is not entirely true. In schools, there are dozens of students in the same grade, with varying levels of intelligence, different hobbies, some liking English, some liking mathematics, some liking Chinese, and some disliking all learning. Therefore, the insights gained from the same book vary greatly among students. Thus, reading in the ["private school style"] is like ["holding the cow's head down to eat grass"], while reading in the ["school style"] is like ["ducks eating snails"], and the drawbacks are not that different? Therefore, those who are good at reading can not only benefit from reading good books, but also benefit from reading bad books. Therefore, Confucius said, ["When walking with two others, I can always find a teacher. I choose their good qualities and follow them, and their bad qualities and correct them"].

In short, it is fine not to read, but if you want to read, the first thing is to ["want"] to. If you ["want"] to, you will be willing to study, and if you are willing to study, you will feel interested, and if you are interested, you will make progress. Therefore, as the saying goes, ["Nothing is difficult in the world for those who put their heart into it"]. If you have a heart for it, then nothing cannot be accomplished. If you don't want to, you will not be willing to study, and if you don't study, where will interest come from? As for whether a person who reads can apply what they learn, that depends on the person. ["There was a person in the Song Dynasty who was good at making a medicine to prevent chapped hands, and his family made a living by washing cotton wadding for generations. A traveler heard of it and bought the recipe for a thousand gold, and used it to persuade the King of Wu, who rewarded him with land and a title"]. This is the difference between being able to apply and not being able to apply.

Page 20

On Children's Literature 291

— Hu Renmu

In recent years, bookstores have been publishing many children's books.

If it is true that these books are published to address the knowledge needs of children, then this phenomenon is commendable. However, to be honest, almost all bookstores publish children's books for profit.

There is nothing wrong with making a profit. Although bookstores are said to be for spreading culture, they naturally must also consider their own business, so making a profit is not a contradictory thing. However, it is very bad to disregard the content of the books because of profit. When we look at the children's books they publish, when we see the intellectual food that these authors bestow upon children, we feel that there are indeed quite a few that we cannot agree with or learn from.

Among these books, those that are of the preaching type are naturally too numerous to mention. In addition, there are many works that go far beyond reality and are completely irrelevant to children's real lives. And the old tune of pigs, dogs, and cows is still being brought out and replayed. If these children's works are simply copied and printed, it seems better not to create or print them.

Children's knowledge should be developed, this is certainly a fact, but before developing their knowledge, one must always consider their proper direction. Like the types of works mentioned above, some want to teach children to become old-fashioned scholars, some are not suitable for children's own environment, and some put them into the group of pigs, dogs, cows, and sheep. I ask, what benefit is there to children? Is this really the right path to develop children's knowledge?

The reason why Ilin's fairy tales are so popular with children in our country and around the world is very simple: it is because he writes about ["children's real lives"]. I think children's literature should pay attention to this point.

The Forgotten Person 292

— Simon

Spending every day in a living circle filled with five-colored lights, metal instruments, the smell of smoke, alcohol, and face powder, the sensory functions gradually become dull. Because the people and things seen every day are truly tiresome and annoying. But one day my senses suddenly returned to their original sensitivity. It was from this day that I discovered a new flower that had been added to the ranks of flowers. 丨丨A young girl, her seat was close to the music stage, in a not very advantageous corner. When she entered this unfamiliar and ever-changing environment on her first night, I paid attention to her. A male leader led her and pointed out her seat, but she did not sit down immediately and hesitated, as if questioning whether she would be spending such days sitting here from today onwards. She stood for a while, and finally sat down.

People, especially all the companions, fixed her with sharp and strange gazes. This made the newcomer, who was completely unaccustomed to that scene, even more uneasy. Her head was lowered slightly, and her eyes stared at the floor, not moving for a long time, sitting there so lonely.

Sitting silently for half a day, a young man came up and she jumped away. While dancing, her eyes still dared not freely glance at the people around her. And her expression was very unnatural. And when the lights came on and the music stopped, a commotion of voices and footsteps arose in the silence. She came back and was confused for a moment, unable to recognize her own seat, but sat down in someone else's seat next to her.

A kind of completely unforgiving sneer immediately burst out of everyone's nostrils. Then a blush flew up her face, all the way to the roots of her ears.

It was common to see her head raised when the lights were off, and when the lights came on, she would quickly look at the floor again. As if afraid of seeing people, and also afraid of being seen by people.

She continued to live so lonely. Every day she dressed as brightly as a night-blooming lily, planted like a flower in countless flower bushes, slipping from the arms of that stranger into the arms of another stranger, using her youthful body and youthful smile to exchange for a little reward. However, it was not necessarily easy to be appreciated. Like her, the number of nights she sat empty was always greater than the number of times someone came to dance with her. Even on the busiest nights at the end of the week, the other companions encountered more soulmates, not a single song was missed, and it was the most enjoyable day of the week.

Everyone was full of energy, smiling happily. But, only she was still sitting coldly, even sitting empty the whole night, no one came to her, no one asked about her. So lonely, she spent her time in vain, watching her companions smile so triumphantly. Then her own face became even more沉 down,沉 down into endless melancholy.

A lonely heart and a forgotten girl!

She was as young as her companions, and painted with the colors of youth and beauty just like them. It was only because the colors of her beauty were covered by a layer of life's shadows丨that they were dulled for no reason.

Often arriving before the others, and similarly often leaving before the others, it was really too lonely. Always sitting there alone. Watching other companions smile and greet the men who came forward, and in the shadow of the lights, hang their chins on the shoulders of the other party, chattering non-stop. Thinking about wanting to please people, even if you try to put on a smiling face, it looks like you're crying, and still no one appreciates that crying smile of hers.

The days fly by quickly, and the days that can be spent in the flower bushes are also very short. And because of excessive worry and the erosion of loneliness, the shadow of depression on her brow became thicker.

There was even less hope for fantasy.

Such a lonely flower, blooming lonely in countless flower bushes, and withering lonely. When it blooms, no one praises it, and when it withers, no one sighs or pities it.

A forgotten person and a lonely heart.

Her coming only made me pay attention, making my senses suddenly keen. Other than that, it seemed that no one else saw her. Now that she has quietly left this place, my keen senses that were caused by her have returned to dullness, and also added a layer of dark clouds that were infected from her loneliness, for her loneliness.

Opening Chapter [Yingying's Prayer]

Yu Xiaoxia Yu Xiaoyun Jade Dragonfly

Xinsheng (1380) 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM

Opening Chapter Hall of Eternal Life [Dreaming]

The sky is pale, geese in rows. Autumn is high, the air is crisp, and the osmanthus is fragrant. Strolling through the flower street, hand in hand in the Royal Garden. Holding a glass of wine in Chenxiang Pavilion. The concubine is scared. The other day, Li Bai went to the Hall of Eternal Life. Compiled Qingping lyrics and composed three pieces. I don't know if the concubine can sing. Waiting for me to listen to the palace business on the clapper. The noble concubine has a gentle and charming voice, and the clapper sounds. With a clever mind and eloquent mouth, there is no match in the world. Jade hand gently pours the dripping wine. Nectar stored in the golden pot. Yang Guifei is drunk, her red complexion is exposed. The palace maids help her onto the ivory bed. Like a painting of a spring sleeping begonia. The Emperor is looking for joy. Suddenly heard the prostitute's fright. Gao Lishi announced the entry of Prime Minister Yang. Guozhong trembles and reports to the Emperor. Tongguan has been breached by the Hu slaves. The rebel soldiers have already entered the Guanxiang. The decree was issued to quickly summon Chen Yuanli. Order him to order troops to protect the Emperor and avoid disaster. The concubine is accustomed to deep palace life. How can tender beauty endure the wind and frost. Moon-like face and flower-like appearance, the road to Shu is long.

One day, Grandma Feng went to Xicheng specifically and happened to meet the sunset glow on the way. At that time, she handed Jiang Qiuwu's letter to her, completing the duties of a matchmaker.

National Studies 299

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Dwelling in Wangchuan Village After Continuous Rain by Wang Wei

Continuous rain in empty woods, smoke and fire late,

Steaming quinoa and cooking millet to feed the eastern plough.

Vast water fields, white egrets fly,

Dense summer woods, yellow orioles turn.

In the mountains, I practice stillness and watch the morning glory,

Beneath the pines, a pure fast, picking dew-covered mallow.

The old farmer has finished arguing for a seat with others,

Why do seagulls still try to imitate me?

Responding to Secretary Guo by Wang Wei

Cave gate high pavilion, the afterglow of the sunset,

Peach and plum shade, willow catkins fly.

Sparse bells in the forbidden palace, the official residence late,

Birds chirping in the province, officials and people few.

In the morning, shaking jade pendants, I hurry to the golden palace,

In the evening, receiving the imperial edict, I bow to the locked gate.

I strongly want to follow you, but I am old and helpless,

I will resign from court because of my illness.

The Shu Chancellor by Du Fu

Where can I find the ancestral hall of the chancellor?

Outside Jin Guan City, cypresses stand tall.

Green grass reflecting the steps, naturally spring colors,

Yellow orioles separated by leaves, empty good sounds.

Thrice he frequently bothered with plans for the world,

Two dynasties he opened and assisted, an old minister's heart.

He died before finishing his expedition,

Forever making heroes weep, tears filling their sleeves.

A Guest Arrives by Du Fu

South and north of my house, all spring waters,

Only seeing flocks of orioles coming day after day.

The flower path has not been swept for guests,

The thatched gate is now opened for you.

The dishes on the plate are far from the market, lacking variety,

The wine in the jug, my family is poor, only old lees.

Willing to drink opposite the neighboring old man,

Calling him over from across the fence to finish the remaining cup.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

The Almost Happened Blindness of Jean Harlow (Part 1) 301

—

What if Jean Harlow, the star of [Wife vs. Secretary] recently shown in this city, went blind? That would certainly be an incredible thing, but not long ago, it was not something absolutely impossible. No one outside has heard about this. Even Jean Harlow herself kept it a secret. It wasn't until recently, when her doctor told her that all danger had passed, that she talked about it with a journalist, and some people outside began to know about it. For the past four years, Jean Harlow has been living in constant fear, afraid that her charming eyes would really go blind. In the past four years, she has also absolutely avoided people talking about this. Only a few close people in her family knew what pain she had suffered in body and spirit in these years!

Now this secret can be made public because her doctor has guaranteed that she will not suffer the pain of blindness. But how did this matter come up again? It was brought about by an accident. Everyone knows that Jean Harlow has some problems with one of her feet. Several years ago, while filming [Hell's Angels], she fell and broke three small bones in her foot. These three small bones have never been properly set, so she often loses her balance and falls. Last month, she fell again, falling from the low wall of her garden. It took almost several weeks for her to walk normally. At that time, a familiar journalist went to visit her, and in the course of the conversation, they talked about her eyes. When the journalist comforted her, Jean said: [What does this count for? The suffering my eyes have endured is much worse.] Jean said, knowing that she had revealed the secret, so she simply told the truth: [I haven't told anyone about this. But now that most of it is in the past, we might as well talk about it. Speaking of which, that incident also happened during the filming of [Hell's Angels]. Do you remember the last section of [Hell's Angels], wasn't it in color? At that time, the method of filming color films was still very primitive. At that time, they were still in the experimental stage. They knew very little. They only knew that when filming color films, the lighting must be three or four times stronger than when filming ordinary films. So all around were filled with arc lights, and there was no place for the actors to walk. I filmed many close-ups. When filming close-ups, many large lights surrounded the sides of the camera. When I was filming, I had to look at the camera with my eyes, and many lights were directly radiating into my eyes. The heat was very high, but I didn't feel it was that high at the time. I filmed close-ups for two consecutive days. Every night when I went home, I felt a splitting headache, unbearable for a moment. I thought at the time that the headache was just caused by overwork of the eyes. But after a few days, my headache became more and more severe. Soon my eyes gradually became inconvenient. I originally had very strong eyesight, but later... I felt blurred and couldn't see clearly.

[Finally, I went to see a doctor. He examined me in detail. His diagnosis was almost unbelievable. He said my eyes were burned. The transparent membrane covering the outside of the eyeballs was scorched by the intense light, just like a person's skin being sunburned by the intense sunlight. Of course, my skin was protected by a thick layer of wax, but my eyes had no protection at all. Of course, this is a strange thing that everyone has never heard of. Even that doctor said it was a very rare thing, but his diagnosis was absolutely true. So he had to start with surgery. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of [Storm] 302

— You Jing

The Storm 丨 Paris Screening

The original play [Thunderstorm] (The Thunderstorm) is one of the famous works among the more than fifty plays by the famous Russian writer Ostrovsky (1823-1886), and it is also a familiar play in the Russian stage repertoire. In the Soviet Union in 1933 after the storm, it was not accidental that this film was made under the significance of critically accepting artistic heritage, reviewing the past life, and showing and building the future.

It should be mentioned here in passing that the Soviet Union's filming of [Circus], [Thunderstorm], and even Maupassant and Balzac's novels should not be superficially understood as the main turning point of Soviet cinema, because this is the same as Hollywood's production tending towards [Nana], [Camille], and [The Count of Monte Cristo], etc. The significance and attitude are different, aren't they? The latter's tendency mainly expresses [the exhaustion of themes] and [the business eye], which is generally recognized. The former is due to the development of film culture 丨 the same as other cultural departments 丨 to a certain stage, reviewing, looking forward, and horizontal photography.

Naturally, after watching [Thunderstorm], you will feel it. It is indeed different from [Road to Life], [The Gold Rush], and [Marionettes]. But this difference does not diminish the significance of the production of [Thunderstorm].

The original author, A., is known as [the master of portraying social figures of that time]. The editors of the film, Fanshibo Chaifu and director Petrov, more faithfully and objectively performed and completed the characters in the play, that is, they typically exposed the people in the social domination of that era.

The old widow's meanness, stubbornness, cruelty, and pretending to be religious 丨 considering it the sin of the daughter-in-law for not bringing 30,000 yuan of dowry, scolding the daughter-in-law and son for embracing when they separated and confided in their grievances as [shameless], ordering the daughter-in-law to swear [never to go near the window to look around, never to peek at any young man;] torturing her by wanting to [bury her alive] etc.

The hypocrisy and flippancy of the merchant class 丨 saying that [all merchants are honest and fair,] the female customer said: [The ruler is better,] but he grabbed her hand and said: [Sweet as chocolate,] and took pride in being ridiculed by his colleagues for [being too gentle with female customers;] casually slapping the young apprentices, and throwing the apprentices on the ground like wood, etc. The selfishness, cruelty, and greed of the merchant's noble son who had attended a higher business school, whose sister attended university, and who inherited one million yuan 丨 when he first came to find Katerina, she refused him with [I am a married woman]. When she finally fled out of the dark family and the custom that [an adulteress must be killed] to ask to go with him to Siberia, he only said [For the sake of my future, I have to work hard] [May God bless you], and abandoned her who had [lived with him for ten nights] and went on horseback to Siberia, etc. And the oppression of Katerina, and the inability to find a way out 丨丨 even the woman who was unwilling to tell a lie to deceive the [great, dear mother-in-law], the girl gave her the key to open the back door to meet her lover, she did not accept it, refused the lover with [a married woman], finally accepted the love of others, and even repented in public, etc., these are the profound and typical descriptions of Russia at the time of [before the storm], what kind of feelings will the people of [after the storm] have when they see it!

Director Petrov in this film, in summary, is messy and somewhat repetitive. But the delicate and everywhere emphasis on the description of the atmosphere of the play is his success. Unlike many Hollywood directors who only pay attention to the acting of the protagonist and neglect the air of the play. In the wedding banquet, the mother-in-law was unhappy because of haggling over the dowry, and the bride only cared about drinking when she told the groom about her past for the first time, and fell asleep on the bed without taking off her boots. These two scenes hinted at the center of the whole play and the character of the characters in the play. That kind of exaggeration of the form of marriage, regardless of whether the content is satisfactory or not, is also deeply meaningful. The capture of dawn, moonlit night, and Volga, etc. formed extremely beautiful pictures. As for the sound effects, it was a great success.

In terms of acting, due to the matching of personality and the proper handling of the director, everyone successfully achieved the degree that should be expressed. Among them, Qieluofu, who played Guderli, was seen by us in [Road to Life]. Although his role here is not as much as that of the villain Fomu Ka in [Road to Life], the deep impression given to people is not reduced to that of other actors.

Review of [Air Hostess] 303

— Ling He

Air Hostess 丨 Cathay

Generally speaking, the themes adopted by American films are indeed very narrow. Horse racing, ball games, boxing matches, boat races, airplanes, and other stimulating themes have been used many times by American film writers. The impression given to people by this phenomenon is that American film themes are lacking. But on the contrary, we also see that they dare not adopt broader themes from the vast crowd, such as in factories and rural areas, there are inexhaustible materials waiting for writers to adopt. So it cannot be said that there is a lack of themes, but that they consciously narrow the scope of themes. As for the application of stimulating materials, there is also the meaning of emphasizing the business eye, which is needless to say.

Now we have seen [Air Hostess] with aviation as the theme again. Regarding this film, we can't find anything except watching a romance between men and women woven into the theme of aviation. Naturally, we can often see this kind of stereotyped story in American movies, and being brave for love here is the most obvious theme of the playwright.

In order to form the love dispute, the appearance of a wealthy and lustful widow is very necessary. Here, as in the methods used in general movies, the widow pours wine on the aviator, goes to the room to change into pajamas, and then the widow sensually seduces him. When the aviator's wife comes to find him, she intentionally wants him to light a cigarette for herself to show her intimacy: these are things that the audience is tired of eating like everyday meals.

Perhaps it can be said that the director's technique is still good, for example, when the two assistants of the female aviator are fighting, they fight very nervously, very like the real thing. In addition, when the female aviator knows that her husband is going to the widow's house, the connecting scenes are also very good. Naturally, this is to say that the director has successfully portrayed the character of a wife who is loyal to love. As for the climax in the back, it is not good.

Golden City Tetralogy 304

— Songhua

The momentum of domestic films seems to have declined a bit recently. In this recent silent air, I suddenly heard that Golden City will continuously release four major domestic blockbusters. Isn't this good news worth reporting? Now, let me briefly introduce the general situation of these four films below.

The Goddess The Goddess film is the latest production of Lianhua Film Company. The main actors are Ruan Lingyu, Li Keng, Zhang Zhizhi, etc. The director is Wu Yonggang. Wu has a very long history in the film industry. Anyone who pays a little attention to the film industry can talk about it. Although it is his first time as a director, the quality of the harvest has exceeded our expectations. This film depicts the general women who groan in hell, who are forced by the environment to engage in this flesh and blood career, but their souls are always pure. The film has a very clear expression of the dual life of such women, the conflict between their conscience and external forces, which is profound and painful, unprecedented. As for the expressions of Ruan Lingyu and Li Keng, etc., of course, they will not disappoint people. This film is scheduled to be released on the 7th (Friday).

The Ordeal of Peach and Plum This is a debut work of the Diantong Company. The achievement of three-friend-style recording has already had a considerable position in the domestic film industry. However, making films themselves is still the first time. And its achievement is unexpectedly excellent, which cannot but be said to be a good phenomenon in domestic films. The content of the film strives to be realistic, depicting a group of young people who are affected by the social depression and the treachery of people's hearts, feel the pain of unemployment, and have a clear indication of the spirit of cooperation between husband and wife. Everything about it is moving in a new direction, which is not comparable to ordinary outdated films. The director is Ying Yunwei, and the main actors are Yuan Muzhi and Chen Bo'er, etc. They all have considerable reputations on the drama stage. Therefore, the performance of [The Ordeal of Peach and Plum] can be said to be amazing.

Flying Flower Village Speaking from the heart, the [Flying Flower Village] film is an excellent production of Yihua Company. Not only is its story tortuous and sad, but also its skills have quite amazing achievements. Zheng Yingshi, this director, his sensitive wrist gave us a very good impression in the [Spring Tide] film. He, directing this [Flying Flower Village] is even more unwilling to relax, so the result is very satisfactory. Furthermore, speaking of Gao Zhanfei's performance, someone has long said that he is progressing rapidly and his future is unlimited. Please wait and see Gao Zhanfei in [Flying Flower Village], and you will definitely be more satisfied. There is also Hu Ping's expression, which has unexpected gains. Wang Naidong's villain is of course worthy of praise.

The Highway This is a major work of Lianhua Company this year. Although the film has not yet been released, the two famous songs in [The Highway], [The Highway Song] and [Pioneer of the Highway], have long been spread in the air of Shanghai. The poet director Sun Yu is the ancestor of changing film styles, and of course he has many new contributions in [The Highway]. All the male stars of Lianhua, Jin Yan, Zheng Junli, Zhang Yi, Zhang Zhizhi, Luo Peng, Han Langen, Shang Guanwu, etc., are all out together, and each is an important role; in addition, there are two female stars, Li Lili and Chen Yanyan, who also joined in the cooperation. We only need to take a look at these many names to guess that it is not an ordinary work. As for the慷慨激昻 of the plot, it is even more rare to see in domestic films.

Wu Lizhu Cries for Li Faxi at Night 305

Under the leadership of director Ren Pengnian, the large team of the Yueming Company was shooting the exteriors of [Delirium] in Suzhou. They brought generators, so even in Jinshanbang, which is far from the city, the lights must be shining at night. Because the actors had no other recreation, they casually came up with some pastimes, which attracted villagers to watch every night, and cheers were thunderous. The heroine Wu Lizhu, who is from Shanghai, often pulled up the Ningbo tune at 10:00 PM when the lights were turned off and cried for the screenwriter Li Faxi. The actresses such as Wu Ling and Chen Peizhu also joined in, so there was a piece of miserable sound, really like someone died, and this was the finale every night before going to bed.

Film Novel

Mother-Daughter Relationship (Lady by Choice) (Part 4) 307

— Zhong Jia

When Pan Xi saw Johnny, she couldn't help but be secretly startled. How could he resemble his father so much? His voice, manner, and smile were just like his father reborn. She thought she would never see that smile or hear that voice again. Seeing him, of course, she couldn't say she didn't know his father. Even if she wanted to pretend, she couldn't. Nor could she say she had forgotten. Forgotten John? Just thinking of his name made her heart ache... Even now... Thinking of their time together... The scenes of them walking together... All those moments spent sitting together in the twilight... She resolutely and proudly refused the weekly allowance that his son offered her... That sum of money that could have freed her from worrying about food and clothing for the rest of her life... All the things she had done in her life were already countless, but she would rather be a beggar than accept a subsidy from John's son. Accepting his subsidy would be like selling the only perfect thing in her life. It would be like taking a price for the sacred love she had generously given to John. So, in the end, she refused Johnny's support, even though Johnny was often worried about her well-being. Now, she had committed a new crime, and Judge Darley was going to call out her old friend's son again, adding to his worries, which made her feel extremely uncomfortable. After a while, Johnny came, and Darley discussed the matter with him in another room. Then, he rushed into the room where Pan Xi was sitting. Pan Xi immediately looked up as she saw them walk in. Darley spoke first: "Pan Xi, Mr. Mills and I have discussed your case. He advised me not to be too hard on you. So, I won't send you to the island. We are going to send you to a nursing home." Johnny's heart couldn't bear to see the sad and bitter look on the old woman's face. Pan Xi suddenly stood up, glaring at them, and said: "I'd rather go to jail!" Her hands were clasped together, expressing the infinite pain in her heart. "That place is where I used to go to do good deeds. It's full of crippled old women sitting in rocking chairs, basking in the sun, knitting wool for a living. Do you think I'll end up like that? I won't! I'm going to tear that place down! I'm going to run away!" But Darley and Johnny didn't listen to her and still sent her to the nursing home. After Pan Xi was sent to the nursing home, she didn't run away, even though the matrons there would have been happy for her to escape, because Pan Xi had already made them helpless in a short time. Suddenly, one day, the whole nursing home was buzzing with excitement, saying that a beautiful young lady was coming to the nursing home to pick out an old woman to be her mother. When Pan Xi heard this, she felt that her chance to escape had come. She was determined that she would be chosen. She looked at the other old women, all dressed up. Some had combs in their hair, some had old lace draped over them, and some had on some worthless ornaments. Pan Xi felt sorry for them, how could they compete with Pan Xi Patterson, who used to be famous on stage? Pan Xi could always perform at any time, and this was of course a good opportunity for her to perform. On that day, the matron indeed led in a beautiful young lady. Pan Xi casually looked up. But unexpectedly, she couldn't help but panic. She seemed to have seen that young lady somewhere before... After thinking about it, she remembered... she had seen her in Darley's midnight court... Her name was Ala Banli, and she was a disreputable fan dancer. Now she was coming to the nursing home to choose an old woman to be her mother—that must be a kind of publicity stunt for them! (To be continued)
